### Added (S-0133 — SWE-hardening Tier 1 closer: Dependabot for pip + github-actions ecosystems)

- **New engine ADR 0069** ([`engine/adr/0069-dependabot-pip-and-actions-ecosystems.md`](adr/0069-dependabot-pip-and-actions-ecosystems.md)) — Dependabot for `pip` (repo-root `pyproject.toml` + `uv.lock` per ADR 0064) and `github-actions` (`.github/workflows/`) ecosystems. Closes [Issue #67](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/67) — **last open SWE-hardening Tier 1 item.** Five coupled decisions: two ecosystems (skip the deprecated `engine/tools/requirements.txt` redirect); weekly Monday cadence (Dependabot default); grouped minor/patch updates per ecosystem (major bumps separate per the contract-change discipline); max 10 open PRs per ecosystem (`affaan-m/everything-claude-code` baseline); auto-rebase on conflict (Dependabot default named explicitly for readability). Plus Conventional Commits via `commit-message.prefix: chore` + `include: scope` → `chore(deps): bump X from A to B`. **Posture clarifications loaded into the ADR (load-bearing against future confusion)**: (A) Dependabot PRs are NOT routine-mode commits — originate from GitHub external apparatus, not `auto_target.json` tasks; routine-mode `scope_lock` does not apply to a Dependabot PR's diff (the routine apparatus never sees the PR). (B) "Intentional-only, no drive-by refreshes" governs human sessions, not Dependabot's cadence — Dependabot IS the intentional refresh procedure, externalized to a weekly schedule. (C) CI (`.github/workflows/validate.yml` per ADR 0065 engine) is the gate for Dependabot PRs; the pre-commit hook lives in local clones and Dependabot's commits originate server-side. (D) Major-version bumps require ADR or amendment if upstream contract changes affect the citing decision; grouped minor/patch is routine. **Cost named explicitly**: Dependabot does NOT regenerate `uv.lock` — pip ecosystem reads `pyproject.toml` floors only; reviewer regenerates the lockfile before merge. PR template's lockfile-regen reminder + CI hard-fail on `uv lock --check` (per ADR 0065 engine decision 3) are the backstops. Trigger criterion evaluation per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md): zero criteria satisfied → **no first-exercise readiness note required** (standard GitHub feature; no novel cross-cutting mechanism). First-PR-arrival empirical verification deferred (~1 week; recorded in a follow-up commit or next session's `outcome_summary`).
- **New [`.github/dependabot.yml`](../.github/dependabot.yml)** — config v2 with two `updates` entries (pip + github-actions), each carrying the same five decisions: weekly Monday cadence, `open-pull-requests-limit: 10`, `rebase-strategy: auto`, `commit-message.prefix: chore` + `include: scope`, and a `pip-minor-and-patch` / `actions-minor-and-patch` group bundling minor + patch update-types. Inline comments name each decision with cross-references to ADR 0069 and the upstream dependency-discipline.md procedures.
- **New "Security-update workflow" rewrite in [`engine/operations/dependency-discipline.md`](operations/dependency-discipline.md)** — past-tense citing ADR 0069 + correction of the prior forward-reference prose. Pre-S-0133 the section claimed Dependabot regenerates `uv.lock`; in fact the pip ecosystem reads `pyproject.toml` floors only. New text: reviewer regenerates lockfile; PR template lockfile-regen reminder; CI hard-fail on `uv lock --check`; no auto-merge (user merges); Dependabot PRs are non-routine; major-version bumps require ADR or amendment; out-of-cadence CVE response via the standard add-a-dep procedure. Interaction-with-other-ADRs row updated from `Issue #67 pending` → `ADR 0069 closes #67`.

### Changed (S-0133 — PR template lockfile-regen reminder + ADR README index)

- **[`.github/PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md`](../.github/PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md) discipline checklist extended** with a new line: `- [ ] If pyproject.toml changed: uv.lock regenerated and staged in the same PR (per ADR 0064; applies to Dependabot PRs — reviewer regenerates before merge per ADR 0069)`. Surfaces the regen step to human reviewers at PR time. Applies symmetrically to human-authored dep changes and Dependabot PRs.
- **[`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md)** index extended with row for ADR 0069; engine count updated from 33 → 34; full ADR collection count updated from 70 → 71 (67 Accepted + 4 Superseded; 34 engine + 37 product).

### Added (S-0132 — SWE-hardening Pairing A: gitleaks + bandit pre-commit/CI security gates)

- **New engine ADR 0067** ([`engine/adr/0067-gitleaks-pre-commit-secret-scanning.md`](adr/0067-gitleaks-pre-commit-secret-scanning.md)) — `gitleaks` pre-commit step (binary version 8.30.1 via `brew install gitleaks`) + GitHub-native secret scanning + push protection. Closes [Issue #66](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/66). Five decisions: pre-commit step before code-discipline gates (`gitleaks protect --staged --config ... --redact --no-banner`); version pin via brew (alternatives `go install` / vendored binary / Python wrapper rejected); project config inherits gitleaks 8.x defaults via `[extend].useDefault = true` + two path-scoped allowlists (`.env.example` forward defense + ADR/operations/build_readiness/ENGINE_LOG paths for canonical fake-secret tokens like `AKIAIOSFODNN7EXAMPLE` cited in documentation); GitHub-native secret_scanning + push_protection enabled (`secret_scanning_non_provider_patterns` + `secret_scanning_validity_checks` deferred); no separate CI gitleaks step (GitHub-native scanning IS the CI-layer). Trigger criterion evaluation per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md): criteria 3 + 4 satisfied → first-exercise readiness note required.
- **New engine ADR 0068** ([`engine/adr/0068-bandit-sast-pre-commit-and-ci.md`](adr/0068-bandit-sast-pre-commit-and-ci.md)) — `bandit` SAST in pre-commit + CI. Closes [Issue #70](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/70). Seven decisions: bandit pinned in `pyproject.toml` (resolved 1.9.4 + stevedore transitive); pre-commit step after code-discipline gates with `uv run bandit -c engine/tools/bandit.yaml -ll -ii -q $STAGED_PY` (`-q` required for non-zero exit on findings); config skips B101 (pytest assert convention) globally + `assert_used.skips` defense-in-depth for test files; gate threshold `-ll -ii` (medium-severity AND medium-confidence floor) — LOW findings (B404 import subprocess, B603 subprocess shell=False default, B607 partial path) are informational only because the engine corpus uses subprocess against system binaries with static args + `env=scrubbed_env()` per [ADR 0045](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md); rule-skip discipline via inline `# nosec BXXX  # reason` annotations (no blanket allowlists); CI extension `.github/workflows/validate.yml` validate job gains `Run bandit SAST on engine/ + product/seed-graph/` step (full-tree, hard-fail); bandit IS in CI (vs gitleaks ISN'T) because GitHub has no SAST-equivalent server-side scan. Trigger criterion evaluation per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md): criteria 3 + 4 satisfied → first-exercise readiness note required.
- **New [`engine/tools/gitleaks.toml`](tools/gitleaks.toml)** — project gitleaks config inheriting defaults + two path-scoped allowlists. Adding a new allowlist entry requires same-session inline comment naming reason per ADR 0067 decision 3.
- **New [`engine/tools/bandit.yaml`](tools/bandit.yaml)** — project bandit config with `skips: [B101]` + `assert_used.skips: ['**/test_*.py', '**/*_test.py']` defense-in-depth. No `exclude_dirs` or `tests` whitelist; inline `# nosec` discipline handles per-finding decisions.
- **New first-exercise readiness note** [`engine/build_readiness/gitleaks_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/gitleaks_first_exercise.md) per ADR 0053. T1-A (pre-commit blocks fake AWS pair on scratch file) + T1-B (`.env.example` path allowlist passes `AKIAIOSFODNN7AAAAAA` placeholder) + T1-C (`gh api -X PATCH` → `secret_scanning.status=enabled` + `secret_scanning_push_protection.status=enabled`, round-trip verified) all closed empirically in-session.
- **New first-exercise readiness note** [`engine/build_readiness/bandit_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/bandit_first_exercise.md) per ADR 0053. T1-A (direct `uv run bandit ... eval(user_input) scratch` → B307 MEDIUM/HIGH, exit 1) + T1-B (CI run [25741717146](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/actions/runs/25741717146) on push of `d7b85ff` concluded `success`) both closed empirically in-session. T1-A's pre-commit-gate path is upstream-blocked by code-discipline test_presence (new `engine/tools/*.py` without companion `test_*.py` rejected before bandit step); direct-invocation evidence is the cleanest empirical verification of the gate.
- **New "External tool prerequisites" subsection in [`engine/operations/dependency-discipline.md`](operations/dependency-discipline.md)** — tabular surface naming `gitleaks` 8.30.1, `gh` (any recent), `uv` (any recent) with brew install paths + ADR pointers. Gate-fail-on-missing discipline + version-pin discipline (major-version drift requires ADR amendment).

### Changed (S-0132 — pre-commit hook + CI workflow extended; pyproject + uv.lock; ADR README index; baseline `# nosec` annotations + SQL refactors)

- **[`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) extended with two new gates.** Gitleaks step after the worktree settings.json sync check (line 165 area), hard-fail on staged-diff secret detection. Bandit step after the code-discipline gates (line 184 area), hard-fail on staged Python findings at `-ll -ii -q` threshold. Both check `command -v` first and emit actionable stderr (brew install / `uv sync` guidance + ADR pointer) on absence. Both re-run with output visible on hard-fail so the maintainer sees the finding details.
- **[`.github/workflows/validate.yml`](../.github/workflows/validate.yml) validate job extended** with `Run bandit SAST on engine/ + product/seed-graph/` step after `Run validate.py --code-gates on changed engine/*.py`. Full-tree scan; hard-fail on findings; top-100 finding lines surfaced to `$GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY` on hard-fail.
- **[`pyproject.toml`](../pyproject.toml)** — `bandit>=1.7.0` added to `[project.dependencies]` matching the ruff/mypy/pytest pattern. **[`uv.lock`](../uv.lock)** regenerated — adds bandit 1.9.4 + stevedore 5.7.0 (transitive).
- **[`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md)** index extended with rows for ADR 0067 + ADR 0068; count updated from 25 to 27 engine ADRs (62 → 64 Accepted total; 25 → 27 engine).
- **[`.env.example`](../.env.example) untouched but tested under the allowlist** (T1-B verified the `.env.example` path-scoped allowlist suppresses placeholder-shaped AWS access keys).
- **Six production tools + four test files annotated with `# nosec BXXX  # reason`** for the 19 of 20 MEDIUM bandit findings on the engine corpus baseline (1 filtered by `-ii` confidence threshold). Production tools: [`engine/tools/audit_mempalace_attribution.py`](tools/audit_mempalace_attribution.py), [`engine/tools/mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py`](tools/mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py), [`engine/tools/prune_mempalace.py`](tools/prune_mempalace.py) (3 sites), [`engine/tools/fetch_structural_reference.py`](tools/fetch_structural_reference.py) (2 sites). Test files: [`engine/tools/test_apply_migration.py`](tools/test_apply_migration.py) (2), [`engine/tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py`](tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py) (3), [`engine/tools/test_probe_session_dir.py`](tools/test_probe_session_dir.py) (1), [`engine/tools/test_prune_mempalace.py`](tools/test_prune_mempalace.py) (5 lines). Three production tools refactored to extract SQL into a named `sql = ...` variable so the `# nosec B608` annotation lives on the line bandit flags (audit_mempalace_attribution.attribute_drawer_metadata, mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.fetch_metadata_rows, prune_mempalace's three SELECT call sites). Shape-preserving — 241 tests pass post-refactor.
- **GitHub repo `security_and_analysis` config flipped** via `gh api -X PATCH repos/StarshipSuperjam/paideia` — `secret_scanning.status` `disabled → enabled`; `secret_scanning_push_protection.status` `disabled → enabled`. Round-trip read verified via `gh api repos/StarshipSuperjam/paideia --jq '.security_and_analysis'`. `dependabot_security_updates` remains `disabled` (separate Tier 1 [Issue #67](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/67) Dependabot adoption); `secret_scanning_non_provider_patterns` + `secret_scanning_validity_checks` remain `disabled` per ADR 0067 decision 4.
- **MemPalace rogue wing `-Users-shanekidd-Documents-Claude-Files-Paideia--claude-worktrees-happy-williams-640cca` (37 drawers) pruned** via `uv run python3 engine/tools/prune_mempalace.py --audit-historical-paths --apply --backup-dir /tmp/mempalace-prune-backup-s0132`. Per the C3 protocol from S-0092: signal-probe-first (37/37 drawers in `room: general`, 37/37 `added_by: mempalace`, zero high-signal `type` / `room: decisions` / `room: lessons` tags), then prune. Backup retained. Pre-prune total: 14,005 drawers; post-prune: 13,968 (-37 exact). `paideia` wing unchanged at 356 drawers. [Issue #2](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/2) (mempalace 3.3.3 wing-name derivation bug, label `upstream`) commented with re-occurrence forensics — the upstream S-0043 fix is incomplete for `.claude/worktrees/<name>` paths (the `.claude` dotfile + worktrees segments may trip the `encoded.rsplit("-", 1)[-1]` logic); Issue stays OPEN.



- **New top-level [`.github/`](../.github/) directory** containing the GitHub Actions workflow and PR template. First `.github/` content for the project; the repo went OSS at S-0130 and S-0131 lands the remote-enforcement layer.
- **New [`.github/workflows/validate.yml`](../.github/workflows/validate.yml)** — two-job CI workflow per [ADR 0065 (engine)](adr/0065-validate-py-mirror-to-ci.md). Triggers: `pull_request` to `main`, `push` to `main`. Job `validate.py` mirrors the pre-commit invocation pattern from [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit): `uv lock --check` (hard-fail in CI per ADR 0065 decision 3, vs soft-warn locally per ADR 0064) → `uv sync --frozen` → default `validate.py` → `validate.py --code-gates --files <changed-py>`. Job `pytest engine/tools` runs the test suite as a separate parallel job — foundation for [Issue #71](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/71) pytest-cov. Both jobs `timeout-minutes: 10` (10-minute hard cap per ADR 0065 decision 4); `astral-sh/setup-uv@v3` cache keyed on `uv.lock` produces ~2.5-minute cold runs, ~30s warm. Soft-warns surface to `$GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY` but exit 0 (preserves the persistent-warn boot surface per [ADR 0042](adr/0042-soft-warn-lifecycle-archive-canon.md)); hard-fails fail the job. CLI-flag discrepancy from Issue #68 body (`--repo-structure --staged --code-gates` doesn't exist as flags) resolved in ADR 0065 — the workflow uses the actual pre-commit pattern.
- **New [`.github/PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md`](../.github/PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md)** — seven-item discipline checklist per [ADR 0066](adr/0066-pr-template-and-branch-protection.md). Adapted from `affaan-m/everything-claude-code`; not verbatim. Sections: Summary, Conventional commit type (with explicit `chore(session):` line for eager-claim commits), discipline checklist (local validate.py / soft-warns / ADR / MemPalace decision drawer / first-exercise readiness note / routine-mode scope_lock / no secrets), Links (ADR / plan file / Closes).
- **New engine ADR 0065** ([`engine/adr/0065-validate-py-mirror-to-ci.md`](adr/0065-validate-py-mirror-to-ci.md)) — Mirror `validate.py` gate to GitHub Actions CI. Closes [Issue #68](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/68). Six decisions: CLI-flag mirror (not Issue body's spec); soft-warns surface but exit-0; `uv lock --check` hard-fail in CI (asymmetric with local soft-warn); 10-minute pipeline budget; routine-mode pushes don't wait for CI (cleanup-signal lives in session-start.sh); judgment patterns from agent-skills `ci-cd-and-automation` (no-skip philosophy, flaky-test fix-not-retry, GitHub Secrets posture). Trigger criterion evaluation per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md): criteria 3 + 4 satisfied → first-exercise readiness note required.
- **New engine ADR 0066** ([`engine/adr/0066-pr-template-and-branch-protection.md`](adr/0066-pr-template-and-branch-protection.md)) — PR template + branch protection on `main`. Closes [Issue #69](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/69). Five decisions: PR template structure; `gh api` invocation (recorded verbatim because GitHub does not expose branch-protection-as-code in repo-tracked YAML); **`enforce_admins=false` load-bearing** (preserves [ADR 0054](adr/0054-lifecycle-push-wrapping-against-default-branch-push-gate.md) `routine_lifecycle_push.py` admin-bypass for unattended routine mode); `required_pull_request_reviews=null` solo-dev (promote when CODEOWNERS lands per [#80](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/80)); multi-commit PR accommodation. Trigger criterion evaluation: none of the four ADR 0053 criteria satisfied → no first-exercise readiness note required (matches Issue #69 body's explicit declaration).
- **New first-exercise readiness note** [`engine/build_readiness/ci_mirror_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/ci_mirror_first_exercise.md) per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) (criteria 3 + 4 satisfied). T1-A (CI green half + CI red half) closed empirically at S-0131 against run [25714935236](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/actions/runs/25714935236) (green) + run [25715091632](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/actions/runs/25715091632) (red on PR [#93](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/pull/93) deliberate-fail). T1-B (first routine-mode push against branch protection) and T1-C (first natural CI-red surfacing via session-start.sh) remain open — await natural exercise.
- **New `[session-start] CI RED on main` LOUD surface in [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh)** (lines after the shared-state health probe block). Reads `gh run list --branch main --limit 1 --json conclusion --jq '.[0].conclusion'` at every boot; emits the LOUD block when conclusion is `failure`. Silent for `success`, empty (no runs yet), `unknown`, or when `gh` is unavailable (legitimate offline-boot). Cleanup-session signal for [ADR 0054](adr/0054-lifecycle-push-wrapping-against-default-branch-push-gate.md) routine pushes that bypass synchronous CI wait.

### Changed (S-0131 — branch protection applied + ADR README index + CI-portability test fixes)

- **Branch protection on `main` applied via `gh api`** per ADR 0066. Required status checks `validate.py` + `pytest engine/tools` with `strict: true`; `required_linear_history: true`; `allow_force_pushes: false`; `allow_deletions: false`; `required_conversation_resolution: true`; `enforce_admins: false`. Round-trip verified via `gh api repos/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/branches/main/protection`.
- **[`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md)** index extended with rows for ADR 0065 (engine) + ADR 0066. Clears two `adr_index_inconsistent` soft-warns surfaced by the first commit of the session.
- **[`engine/tools/conftest.py`](tools/conftest.py)** extended with autouse `_scrub_project_env` fixture that strips `SUPABASE_DB_URL` at every test start. Closes a leak path from `test_load_env.test_load_dotenv_walk_up_finds_main_repo_env_from_worktree` (monkeypatch.delenv-after-direct-os.environ-assign undo semantics) that broke `test_validate.TestMain.test_default_mode_clean_returns_non_two` on Ubuntu CI runners (the leaked `postgresql://test` URL caused `validate.main()` to attempt a DNS lookup that hard-failed, flipping the test's expected exit-1 to exit-2). Per-test `monkeypatch.setenv` in legitimate consumers still wins because per-test setenv runs after the autouse fixture.
- **[`engine/tools/test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`](tools/test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py) and [`engine/tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py)** — both `_make_origin_with_clone` helpers now pass `--initial-branch=main` to `git init --bare`. Closes a CI-portability path where runners with `init.defaultBranch=master` (GitHub Actions default) left the bare origin's HEAD pointing at a nonexistent `master` ref after the local clone pushed `main`. The mismatch silently broke `git reset --hard HEAD~1` in 4 `test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py` tests (loser-clone setup) and `test_push_failure_non_fast_forward_returns_3` in `test_routine_lifecycle_push.py` (assert 0 == 3 because the push that should have been rejected silently succeeded). Requires git ≥ 2.28; CI ships 2.53.
- **[`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md)** Last build session row replaced with S-0131; SWE-hardening rollout table marks #68 + #69 as closed and removes the now-obsolete blockers from #67 / #70 / #71. ADR count corrected from 66 to 68 (62 → 64 Accepted; 29 → 31 engine).

- **Repository visibility flipped from PRIVATE to PUBLIC** via `gh repo edit StarshipSuperjam/paideia --visibility public --accept-visibility-change-consequences`. Post-flip `gh repo view --json visibility,licenseInfo` reports `visibility: PUBLIC`, `licenseInfo.key: apache-2.0`, `licenseInfo.name: Apache License 2.0` — GitHub Licensee correctly identifies the canonical Apache 2.0 LICENSE text. Annotated tag `oss-flip-v1.0.0` created against the Phase G post-pass commit (`65376d4`) with message *"OSS visibility flip — Apache 2.0 source open per ADR 0065 (S-0130)"* and pushed to origin. STATE.md GitHub row updated from `(private)` to `(OSS, Apache 2.0; public-flip landed at S-0130 with tag oss-flip-v1.0.0)`. The flip closed the OSS+BYOK three-session sequence (S-0128 / S-0129 / S-0130) that began with ADR 0065 supersession of ADRs 0029 + 0035 at S-0128. Repo URL `https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia` is now indexable, forkable, and discoverable; the milestone-bound repo-migration trigger (ADR 0065 commitment 7 — migrate to org account before first App Store submission) remains pending at the Phase 9 boundary. Executed at session close after user explicit `go` authorization per the locked plan halt-and-confirm gate.

### Changed (S-0130 — OSS pivot + BYOK refactor Session C: LICENSE relicense + OSS+BYOK posture rewrites + 141-file PII sweep)

- **[`LICENSE`](../LICENSE) replaced** with the canonical Apache License 2.0 text verbatim (202 lines from `https://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0.txt`). Prior content was a proprietary "all rights reserved" notice; the relicensing matches ADR 0065 commitment 7 (source open under Apache 2.0 with attribution to "The Paideia Project Contributors"). The project copyright lives in [`NOTICE`](../NOTICE) per standard Apache 2.0 convention, keeping the LICENSE file as the unmodified canonical text for license-detector recognition (GitHub Licensee, SPDX tooling).
- **[`SECURITY.md`](../SECURITY.md) rewritten** for OSS+BYOK posture. Project-status section replaces the prior private-pre-launch framing with OSS + personal-project + no-commercial-SLA. Reporting section routes vulnerabilities through GitHub's private-advisory channel. **BYOK posture subsection** (load-bearing) anchors on ADR 0065 commitment 8 verbatim — *"The user's Anthropic API key lives only on-device in iOS Keychain. No Paideia-controlled server receives the key, proxies the API, or observes the API exchange."* — plus iOS Keychain storage with `kSecAttrAccessibleWhenUnlockedThisDeviceOnly` and no iCloud sync, plus the maintainer-side back-end (Supabase + engine tooling) clarification that graph construction / analysis / aggregated mastery-state ingestion never receives user API keys. Scope rewrite covers credential exposure in tracked files / graph data (Supabase) / engine-side build tooling / iOS app surface (Phase 6+) / MemPalace. Out-of-scope rewrites cover third-party platform security (Anthropic, Supabase, Apple) defer-to-upstream + Phase 6+ unreleased surfaces.
- **[`README.md`](../README.md) rewritten** in three targeted edits. Status line replaces "design and early implementation; Phase 3 deployed" with "OSS (Apache 2.0) — pre-Phase-6 personal project, post-pivot from cost-capped pseudo-SaaS to BYOK direct-API (per ADR 0065). App Store distribution pending the Phase 9 milestone. Contributions accepted at maintainer discretion." Repository line drops `(private)`. Repo-map block adds `NOTICE` / `CONTRIBUTING.md` / `CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md` rows, and the LICENSE row's parenthetical updates from the prior proprietary-with-personal-name annotation to `Apache License 2.0 (see NOTICE for copyright)`. License section at the bottom replaces "Proprietary, all rights reserved" with "[Apache License 2.0]" + Contributors copyright reference + the App-Store-fork-rebrand discipline + pointer to [`CONTRIBUTING.md`](../CONTRIBUTING.md).
- **[`.env.example`](../.env.example) annotated** with a BYOK comment block prepended at file head. Explicitly states: the iOS app does NOT consume this file under BYOK; users provide their Anthropic API key via in-app onboarding into iOS Keychain; the app does not read from `.env` at any point. Variables below the block are for engine-side scripts (`validate.py` graph audit, health-check tooling, MemPalace) — maintainer-only. Existing variable list unchanged.
- **[`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) Phase C path cleanup**. Moved the seven main-repo-path-dependent git permission patterns from tracked `.claude/settings.json` (former lines 4–10, which hardcoded the maintainer's absolute home-prefixed Paideia path) to gitignored `.claude/settings.local.json`. Tracked `.claude/settings.json` is now portable across machines; per-clone `settings.local.json` carries the path-specific permissions. Per-clone setup: new contributors / new machines populate their own `settings.local.json` equivalent. Verified by post-cleanup grep against the absolute-path prefix returning zero hits in the tracked file.

Substitution applied to replace the maintainer's absolute home-prefix with the home-relative `~/` shorthand across every tracked file that contained it. The `engine/session/current.json` `worktree` field was rewritten from absolute to tilde form alongside the 129 prior archives, matching the privacy-preserving intent of the sweep.

### Changed (S-0129 — OSS pivot + BYOK refactor Session B: downstream doc rewrites)

- **[`product/docs/business.md`](../product/docs/business.md)** rewritten against [ADR 0065](../product/adr/0065-oss-pivot-and-byok-disposition.md). Personal Project Disposition section's commitment list grew from six commitments to eight (Apple platforms + SwiftUI codebase preserved verbatim; subscription → free download + one-time IAP unlock; builder-eats-API-costs → infrastructure-only floor; no-BYOK → consumer-BYOK with institutional foreclosure preserved; cost-ceiling mechanism retires; static polish preserved with threat-shape inversion noted; new Apache 2.0 source commitment; new on-device Keychain key-handling commitment). Pricing and Distribution table rewritten — subscription rows removed, free download + IAP unlock + free-tier-as-structural-affordance + BYOK row added, IAP dollar amount TBD. Operating Cost Model retitled to "Infrastructure Operating Cost" — single-part floor (~$200–300/yr) independent of user count; no Paideia revenue path that recovers API cost. Annual Operating Subsidy Budget section retired entirely. Cost Amplification with Session Length reframed from builder-perspective to user-perspective (helps the user manage their own Anthropic bill). Cancellation Discipline extended — OSS source survives App Store binary cancellation; Anthropic credential is user-held, not Paideia-held.
- **[`product/docs/infrastructure.md`](../product/docs/infrastructure.md)** Deployment Target section rewritten — Apple-only deployment (iPhone + iPad first-class via SwiftUI; Mac via Designed-for-iPad); user iOS app calls Anthropic API directly with the user's BYOK; no proxy. Dropped Native iOS/Android framing, web-app-as-test-surface, sideloading-option sub-bullets. New "BYOK key handling" subsection added — Keychain storage with `kSecAttrAccessibleWhenUnlockedThisDeviceOnly`; no iCloud Keychain sync; no key in logs / crash reports / telemetry; force-crash pre-submission test (Apple guideline 5.1.1); names what does and does not run on the user's device (graph build / graph analysis are back-end maintainer work; user conversations surface signals that the back-end review pipeline consumes as candidate inputs, like bug reports vs. code patches). Cloud Hosting Stack section clarifies build-tooling vs user-app data paths. Cost Mitigation Ideas retitled to "User Cost Mitigation Patterns" and reframed user-side; pedagogical-degradation discipline named as the qualitative guardrail. New "See also" section pointing to ADRs 0065 / 0026 / 0014.
- **[`ROADMAP.md`](../ROADMAP.md) Phase 8 (Evaluation Harness)** success criteria rewritten — cost-cap-mechanism criterion removed; user-facing BYOK onboarding flow + Keychain storage + `/v1/messages` round-trip validation added; force-crash pre-submission test added (Apple guideline 5.1.1); milestone-bound repo-migration trigger added (Phase-9-entry gate per [ADR 0065](../product/adr/0065-oss-pivot-and-byok-disposition.md) commitment 7); privacy questionnaire criterion extended ("data not collected" for the API credential per commitment 8); cold-test now exercises the BYOK onboarding flow alongside the teaching surface. See-also list drops ADR 0029 / ADR 0035 (superseded), adds ADR 0065.
- **[`ROADMAP.md`](../ROADMAP.md) Phase 9 (UI Prototype)** success criteria rewritten — cost-cap-mechanism-against-production criterion replaced with the pedagogical-degradation discipline per [ADR 0014](../product/adr/0014-sonnet-teaches-opus-reviews.md) (absorbed from retired ADR 0029); BYOK onboarding flow added as a first-class UI primitive alongside delete-account, data-export, and exit affordance; static-polish foreclosure extended (funnel-mechanic discipline now binds against user-funnel-mechanic alongside builder-funnel-mechanic per [ADR 0065](../product/adr/0065-oss-pivot-and-byok-disposition.md)); supersession reference updated from "requires superseding ADR 0035" to "requires superseding ADR 0065." See-also list drops ADR 0029 / ADR 0035 (superseded), adds ADR 0065.
- **[`ROADMAP.md`](../ROADMAP.md) Strong working commitments item 2** updated to point at [ADR 0065](../product/adr/0065-oss-pivot-and-byok-disposition.md) with the chain preserved through superseded predecessors ([ADR 0032](../product/adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md), [ADR 0035](../product/adr/0035-multi-platform-apple-expansion.md), [ADR 0029](../product/adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md)).
- **[`product/docs/MISSION.md`](../product/docs/MISSION.md) Disposition paragraph** rewritten — open-source under Apache 2.0; free-download-with-IAP-unlock under the maintainer's personal Apple Developer account; users supply their own Anthropic key (BYOK) stored on-device in Keychain. Freshman-defaults calibration now also applies to the in-app BYOK key-onboarding flow. Refusal-not-deferral foreclosure preserved verbatim; ADR pointer updated from 0032 → 0065. Strong working commitment 2 rewrites — threat shape binds against user-funnel-mechanic alongside builder-funnel-mechanic; the same discipline answers both; structural free-tier permitted as affordance, not conversion funnel; ADR chain preserved through superseded predecessors. Items 1, 3–12 unchanged.
- **[ADR 0014](../product/adr/0014-sonnet-teaches-opus-reviews.md) Consequences extended** with the absorbed pedagogical-degradation principle from the retired [ADR 0029](../product/adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md) cost-ceiling mechanism — *degrade rather than terminate mid-concept-engagement* — recorded as a teaching discipline scoped to Sonnet's per-turn context preparation (retrieval-window downshifts, two-hop → one-hop neighborhood); Opus's batch-review aggregation unaffected. OQ-WALL-BEHAVIOR closure framing carried into ADR 0014's Consequences body. ADR 0014 Status unchanged (Accepted) — Consequences extension, not Decision revision. See-also rows updated for the superseded predecessors and the new ADR 0065.

### Added (S-0128 — OSS pivot + BYOK refactor Session A)

- **New product ADR 0065** ([`product/adr/0065-oss-pivot-and-byok-disposition.md`](../product/adr/0065-oss-pivot-and-byok-disposition.md)) — supersedes [ADR 0029](../product/adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md) (personal financial cost ceiling) and [ADR 0035](../product/adr/0035-multi-platform-apple-expansion.md) (multi-platform Apple expansion). Commits an eight-commitment disposition: (1) Apple platforms via App Store preserved verbatim; (2) free download + one-time IAP unlock replacing the cost-priced subscription (dollar amount deferred to Phase 8/9 implementation session per user); (3) builder operating cost retires to infrastructure-only floor (~$200–300/yr) — users pay Anthropic directly; (4) consumer BYOK adopted with in-app onboarding flow mitigating the freshman-self-selection concern, institutional BYOK / licensing / grants / acquisition foreclosed unchanged; (5) cost-ceiling mechanism per ADR 0029 retires (no Paideia-controlled API account exists under BYOK); (6) static polish / minimum-shape maintenance preserved verbatim; (7) [new] source open under Apache 2.0 with attribution to "The Paideia Project Contributors"; (8) [new] user's API key lives only on-device in iOS Keychain, server stays key-blind via [ADR 0026](../product/adr/0026-persistent-learner-storage-structural-not-substantive.md)'s transcript-non-persistence guarantee. Apple App Store compliance posture committed in advance (Guidelines 5.1.1 / 4.0 / 3.1.1 / 3.2.2). Milestone-bound repo-migration trigger recorded (migrate `StarshipSuperjam/paideia` → org account before first App Store submission). Trademark on "Paideia" deferred-reactive. Session A is the contract commit; Session B (S-0129) does downstream doc rewrites; Session C (S-0130) does LICENSE / PII cleanup / OSS hygiene / public-flip per the approved plan at [`~/.claude/plans/i-want-to-shift-hidden-hedgehog.md`](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia).
- **MemPalace `decision` drawer** filed in `wing_paideia/decisions` topic "OSS pivot plus BYOK disposition; supersedes ADRs 0029 + 0035 (S-0128, ADR 0065)" (id `drawer_paideia_decisions_cb5585958acc4043495228dc`). Captures the conversational reasoning verbatim — entanglement of OSS+BYOK shifts; artifact-survival motivation rather than commercial pivot; license choice (Apache 2.0) reasoning; the mechanism-vs-justification amend-vs-supersede discipline pair with the S-0012 ADR 0029 amendment drawer (S-0012 = justification-changes-amends; S-0128 = mechanism-changes-supersedes); user-adjudicated decisions (attribution to "The Paideia Project Contributors"; keep `StarshipSuperjam/paideia` with milestone-bound migrate trigger; defer specific pricing; defer trademark filing); the rejected-alternatives slate (backend proxy for key-handling; MIT/MPL/AGPL for license; three-separate-supersession-ADRs vs one).

Closes Issue [#65](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/65); unblocks downstream Tier 1 SWE-hardening Issues #67 / #68 / #69 / #70 / #71.

- **New `uv.lock` at repo root** — 99 packages resolved; 439KB / 2290 lines.
- **New ops doc [`engine/operations/dependency-discipline.md`](operations/dependency-discipline.md)** — Layer 1 source-of-truth for dependency lifecycle: source-of-truth surface table, install procedure, refresh procedure (intentional-only), add/remove dep procedures, security-update workflow, validator soft-warn semantics, ADR cross-references, S-0127 migration notes.
- **New validator soft-warn `uv_lock_out_of_date`** in [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py): runs `uv lock --check` (cwd=repo-root); non-zero exit emits the warn. Three no-op cases for non-adopted clones (missing pyproject / lockfile / `uv` binary). Lives in the `health_probe` phase per ADR 0063 (subprocess to `uv`).
- **New first-exercise readiness note** [`engine/build_readiness/uv_lockfile_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/uv_lockfile_first_exercise.md) per ADR 0053 (criteria 2, 3, 4 satisfied — new soft-warn category, new state file, ≥3 ops docs / ≥5 tooling files affected). T1-A closed at authoring; T1-B/C/D await natural exercise.
- **6 new pytests** at [`engine/tools/test_validate.py::TestValidateUvLockFreshness`](tools/test_validate.py) covering the four no-op shapes (absent pyproject / absent lockfile / absent `uv` binary / subprocess timeout) and the clean + stale-fire paths.
- **MemPalace `decision` drawer** filed in `wing_paideia/decisions` topic "S-0127 ADR 0064 — uv lockfile + reproducible builds (Issue #65)" capturing the five coupled decisions, considered-and-rejected alternatives (PEP 735 dependency-groups deferred; uv version pinning deferred; hard-fail rejected; structural-phase placement rejected during exercise; pilot framing rejected per feedback memory), and verification record.

### Changed (S-0127 — Issue #90 four-phase validator model)

- **ADR 0063 contract-folded** ([`engine/adr/0063-validator-tiered-runtime-targets-and-regression-soft-warn.md`](adr/0063-validator-tiered-runtime-targets-and-regression-soft-warn.md)) for the four-phase model per ADR 0036 (no inline `### Amendment` block). Decision section names four phases: structural / health_probe / graph_audit / total. New Consequences entry records the S-0127 split with rationale (subprocess-to-external-system is categorically different from in-memory contract checks). Closes Issue [#90](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/90).
- **`VALIDATOR_PHASE_TARGETS_MS`** updated: added `duration_health_probe_ms = 5000.0`; bumped `duration_total_ms` from 6000.0 → 11000.0 to accommodate the new phase + ~500ms buffer for `--final-check` shutdown audits.
- **`validate.py main()` refactored** for the four-phase model. `validate_shared_state_health()` AND `validate_issue_collisions()` both moved out of structural into the new health_probe phase (both spawn subprocesses to live external systems — chromadb open via `probe_palace.py` and `gh issue list` respectively). New `t_health_probe_end` boundary; `duration_health_probe_ms` field emitted to `validate-history.jsonl` records.
- **`validate_uv_lock_freshness` (new) wired into the health_probe phase** in `validate.py main()` after the two prior probes; tested at first cut as a structural-phase placement and moved per the same conceptual definition (subprocess to external tool = health_probe).
- **First-exercise T1-B for `validator_runtime_phase_regression` closed via Path B** (phase boundary correction with evidence) at [`engine/build_readiness/validator_runtime_phase_regression_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/validator_runtime_phase_regression_first_exercise.md). The S-0126 first-fire surfaced ~3700ms `duration_structural_ms`; investigation confirmed `validate_shared_state_health` (~3500ms) + `validate_issue_collisions` (~700ms) as the contributors. Path A (chromadb optimization) and threshold-bump fallback both rejected on principled grounds; the four-phase split is the right resolution.
- **3 ADR 0063 test updates + 3 new tests** at [`engine/tools/test_validate.py::TestValidateRuntimePhaseRegression`](tools/test_validate.py): `_clean_entry` and `_breaching_entry` helpers extended for four phases; existing tests retain coverage; new tests added for `phase_targets_dict_has_four_phases`, `only_health_probe_phase_breaches_fires_single_warn`, and `pre_split_three_phase_entries_skipped`. Total 12 tests in the class (was 9).
- **`engine/tools/health_check.py audit_fit` runtime summarizer** extended to median-print `duration_health_probe_ms` alongside structural and graph_audit medians. Tiered-target reference updated to four phases (structural < 500ms; health probe < 5s; graph audit < 5s; total < 11s).
- **`engine/operations/health-check.md` Validator-telemetry section** updated to four phases.
- **`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`** — Response-posture section's runtime-budget bullet updated to four phases; `validator_runtime_phase_regression` entry updated to reflect the S-0127 fold and the phase-boundary-correction recoverability path; new `uv_lock_out_of_date` category entry authored; classification map extended (42 rows; new rows for `validator_runtime_phase_regression` and `uv_lock_out_of_date` under Actively-tracked, deferred re-audit).

### Added (S-0126 — close S-0121 audit follow-ups #87 #88 #89)

- **New engine ADR 0062** ([`engine/adr/0062-retire-adr-inline-amendments-and-governed-doc-soft-warns.md`](adr/0062-retire-adr-inline-amendments-and-governed-doc-soft-warns.md)) — retires the ADR Consequences inline-amendment pattern + mechanizes three governed-doc soft-warns. - **New engine ADR 0063** ([`engine/adr/0063-validator-tiered-runtime-targets-and-regression-soft-warn.md`](adr/0063-validator-tiered-runtime-targets-and-regression-soft-warn.md)) — replaces the unitary `< 500ms` validator runtime target with tiered targets (structural < 500ms / graph audit < 5s / total < 6s) + per-phase timing instrumentation + `validator_runtime_phase_regression` soft-warn. - **Four new validator soft-warns** in [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py):
  - `state_md_row_count` — threshold 180 rows (baseline 118 at S-0126); per ADR 0062.
  - `adr_consequences_amendment_header` — zero-tolerance pattern catch on `### Amendment` headers in any ADR file; per ADR 0062.
  - `handoff_long_resolved_sections` — threshold 5 total OR any section >10 sessions old; per ADR 0062.
  - `validator_runtime_phase_regression` — fires when any phase exceeds 1.5× target across 3 consecutive runs; per ADR 0063.
- **Per-phase timing instrumentation** in `validate.py` main(): `duration_structural_ms`, `duration_graph_audit_ms`, `duration_total_ms` in `validate-history.jsonl` records. Prior `duration_ms` renamed cleanly to `duration_total_ms`; `health_check.py` reader accepts both shapes for cross-S-0126 history continuity.

  - [`engine/build_readiness/governed_doc_soft_warns_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/governed_doc_soft_warns_first_exercise.md) covering the three governed-doc soft-warns (T1-A: first natural fire; T1-B: corrective edit motivated).

Filed as a follow-up Issue for downstream investigation.

- **Three GitHub Issues filed for accepted S-0121 audit findings** ([Issue #87](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/87) / [#88](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/88) / [#89](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/89), all `health-check-finding + tech-debt`):

Bundled because all four share the *AI-default additive prose authorship in governed documents* root pattern; adding the soft-warns IS the mechanization half of Retire-C's (b). 8 ADRs affected (0042/0045/0047/0048/0049/0054/0056/0057). ADR + decision drawer + first-exercise readiness note required.
  - **#88** — retire stale `< 500ms` validator runtime target (per [ADR 0016](adr/0016-graph-construction-needs-live-validation.md) Phase 4 added live-DB graph audit; current ~4.25s reflects the consultation cost). Replace with tiered targets (structural < 500ms, graph-audit < 5s, total < 6s) + per-phase timing instrumentation in `validate.py` + `validate-history.jsonl` schema extension.
  - **#89** — refine `scan_orphans.py` `ops-doc-uncited` axis against false-positives. Audit found 19 of 22 ops docs flagged but all carry 18–63 inbound file references and are load-bearing (consumed-by-behavior, not literally cited in `outcome_summary`). Tightening: file-reference threshold (<10 inbound) OR boot-surface reachability check.

### Added (S-0123 — Phase 5 production-audit follow-up migrations)

- **[`product/seed-graph/migrations/0061_seed_historical_influence_retyping_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0061_seed_historical_influence_retyping_part1.sql)** — first follow-up migration. Retypes 17 history-terminator-source edges from `pedagogical_prerequisite` to `historical_influence` per [ADR 0061 product](../product/adr/0061-historical-influence-retyping-for-history-terminator-bridges.md): 14 cross-bridges A3 grouping (CB-E-28 through CB-E-43 sourced from `aristotelian_four_causes` / `greek_atomism` / `scholasticism` / `renaissance_mechanism` / `vienna_circle_logical_positivism`); 2 within-service A3-internal (`presocratic_naturalism → aristotelian_four_causes`; `aristotelian_four_causes → vienna_circle_logical_positivism`); 1 within-mind (`consciousness → phenomenology`). **First-use of the `historical_influence` predicate** (registered in v1 PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md since schema's initial draft, zero edges using it before). Implementation chose UPDATE in place over DELETE+INSERT because the schema commits a single `public.edges` table per `0003_edges.sql` (no per-predicate table; ADR 0061 prose left the schema-name open per "PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md is the source of truth"). UPDATE preserves the original UUID `id`, `created_at`, and `graph_version_added=16`. Each UPDATE populates `evidence` with the audit's verdict reasoning. Layer 2.5 assertions: 5 declared, all passed at apply time. Closes Issue [#60](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/60).
- **[`product/seed-graph/migrations/0062_seed_direction_flips_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0062_seed_direction_flips_part1.sql)** — second follow-up migration. Flips direction on 15 reversed `pedagogical_prerequisite` edges per S-0122 findings §"Reversal cluster" + §"Direction-of-development reversal patterns": 8 cross-bridges B reversal cluster + 7 within-subdomain reversals. Implementation: UPDATE in place swapping `source_id` and `target_id`. Pre-apply audit confirmed zero canonical-direction collisions. Layer 2.5 assertions: 4 declared, all passed at apply time. **Cycle deferral**: the CB-E-63 flip (`proposition → propositional_attitude`) closed a 4-node Kosaraju cycle through pre-existing edges (`intentionality → meaning → proposition → propositional_attitude → intentionality`, where the back-edge from `0040` was audit-accepted). Per S-0123 user adjudication via AskUserQuestion (option "Revert CB-E-63 only"), the flip was reverted in `0062_seed_direction_flips_revert_part1.sql`. The 4-node cluster re-scope is deferred to Phase 6 audit infrastructure (Issue [#64](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/64)). Net effect: 14 of 15 audit-mandated flips stand. Closes Issue [#59](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/59) modulo the CB-E-63 deferral.
- **[`product/seed-graph/migrations/0062_seed_direction_flips_revert_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0062_seed_direction_flips_revert_part1.sql)** — companion revert migration. Reverts only CB-E-63 (`proposition → propositional_attitude` back to `propositional_attitude → proposition`); evidence column populated with a cycle-deferral note cross-referencing Issue #64. Layer 2.5 assertions: 4 declared, all passed at apply time. Total `pedagogical_prerequisite` count remains 519; cycle cleared.
- **[`product/seed-graph/migrations/0063_seed_weak_edge_cleanup_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0063_seed_weak_edge_cleanup_part1.sql)** — third follow-up migration. Two operations: (A) PRUNE 4 weak/redundant edges where the more-proximate canonical prereq is already in graph (CB-E-5, CB-E-27, MET-E-10, LOG-E-7); (B) ANNOTATE 5 retain-with-annotation edges with their alliance/pressure rationale (CB-E-67, ETH-E-17, ETH-E-20, EPI-E-2, EPI-E-20). Layer 2.5 assertions: 4 declared, all passed at apply time. Total `pedagogical_prerequisite` reduced 519 → 515 (-4 prunes); total edges reduced 536 → 532. Closes Issue [#61](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/61).
- **[`product/seed-graph/migrations/0064_seed_evidence_annotations_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0064_seed_evidence_annotations_part1.sql)** — fourth follow-up migration. Backfills evidence on 7 defensible-with-annotation edges per S-0122 Disposition matrix (defensible/documentation verdicts): MET-E-3, MET-E-12, MIN-E-12, LAN-E-3, LAN-E-5, POL-E-6, AES-E-3. Distinct from 0063's retain-with-annotation set (weak/parallel-edge category) — 0064's set is from the defensible-with-annotation category where the pedagogical-prereq framing encodes a specific dialectical / metaontological / framework commitment. Layer 2.5 assertions: 3 declared, all passed at apply time. Closes Issue [#63](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/63).
- **GitHub Issue [#64](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/64)** filed — re-scope CB-E-63 direction flip alongside the 4-node `intentionality / meaning / proposition / propositional_attitude` cluster. Defers the CB-E-63 audit-mandated correction pending Phase 6 audit infrastructure's holistic re-scope of the cluster (since flipping CB-E-63 alone closes a cycle through the audit-accepted `propositional_attitude → intentionality` edge from `0040`).

Hub identification by parametric scan of the 15 Phase 5 seed migrations: classical_logic (logic, deg 9 — 3 out + 6 in), meaning (language, deg 9 — 7 out + 2 in), normative_ethics (ethics, deg 9 — 8 out + 1 in), vienna_circle_logical_positivism (service, deg 9 — 6 out + 3 in), aristotelian_four_causes (service, deg 8 — 7 out + 1 in). Sample density: 100% on incident edges per master-plan §"Sample-size policy" hubs row. Edge-verdict tally: 26 sound (22 sound-high + 4 sound-medium) + 1 defensible-medium (E-5 bivalence_principle → classical_logic system-vs-defining-principle ordering) + 17 historical-not-pedagogical-high (E-28 through E-43 minus E-34 inter-hub dedupe — covering ALL 17 incident edges of the two history-terminator hubs uniformly: 6 outgoing from vienna_circle_logical_positivism + 3 incoming to vienna_circle_logical_positivism with E-34 inter-hub + 7 outgoing from aristotelian_four_causes minus the dedupe + 1 incoming to aristotelian_four_causes) + 1 weak-high (E-18 philosophy_of_language → meaning discipline-label-as-prereq, structurally redundant; cross-references master-plan §"Audit-system-input proposals" #2 candidate). Node-verdict tally: 1 sound-high (N-2 meaning) + 1 sound-medium (N-1 classical_logic with granularity-overlap-with-constituent-prop/predicate-logic flag) + 1 granularity-mismatch-medium (N-3 normative_ethics — sub-discipline-label boundary case, 1 in-edge so doesn't strictly fire §"Audit-system-input proposals" #2 zero-in-edges precondition but is shape-similar to philosophy_of_language) + 2 granularity-mismatch-high (N-4 vienna_circle_logical_positivism literal master-plan school-name example; N-5 aristotelian_four_causes literal master-plan thinker-framework example). Substantive-defect rate at edge level: **18/43 = 41.9%** — high, driven by the history-terminator hub concentration. **Bimodal pattern at hub level**: concept-level hubs (HUB F + G + H, 27 edges) at 1/27 = 3.7% defect rate; history-terminator hubs (HUB I + J, 17 edges) at 17/17 = 100% defect rate. Combined with S-0119's hub-centrality finding (top-5 hubs 87% sound at edge level), the hub-centrality defense-side finding extends with HUB-SHAPE-CONDITIONAL refinement: concept-level hubs are even MORE sound than the S-0119 top-5 (96% vs 87%); history-terminator hubs are uniformly defective. **Three pattern-aggregation surfaces strengthened for the closeout**: (1) HISTORICAL_INFLUENCE PREDICATE-ACTIVATION cumulative count further strengthened — 17 incident-edge findings from this fire alone, on top of S-0081 gate's ~19 + S-0104's 14 + S-0116's within-service findings + S-0119's E-43 + E-53 (2 cross-bridge-from-history-terminator findings); cumulative ≥48+ historical-not-pedagogical findings, comfortably exceeding the master-plan §"Structural reopen pre-flag" 10+ ADR-warranting threshold with WIDE margin; closeout's expected disposition (activate `historical_influence` predicate; retype affected edges) has decisive evidence. (2) `discipline_label_node_at_root` proposal scope question — this fire surfaces three nodes at the discipline-label boundary (philosophy_of_language E-18 zero-in-edges fires the proposal as currently formulated; normative_ethics N-3 1 in-edge doesn't strictly fire but is shape-similar; ontology and metaphysics TRACE 2 terminals at depths 4–5 not under per-node review here but flagged); proposal precondition (zero-in-edges) may be too narrow; closeout adjudicates whether to loosen to "few-in-edges + many-out-edges-to-domain-concepts". (3) HUB-SHAPE-CONDITIONAL hub-centrality finding — concept-level hubs concentrate substantive soundness; history-terminator hubs concentrate substantive defects. **Trace findings**: TRACE 1 gettier_problem mostly sound, missing fallibilism prereq; TRACE 2 modal_realism sound but with discipline-label terminals at depths 4–5; TRACE 3 social_contract_theory partially defensible — depth-1 expected_value too-narrow Rawlsian-decision-theoretic-only, depth-1 political_philosophy is discipline-label-as-prereq, canonical antecedents (state_of_nature, political_obligation, political_legitimacy, consent, natural_rights) absent from the depth-3 chain; CANDIDATE STRUCTURAL FINDING: social_contract_theory's prereq structure under-represents the political-theory pedagogical lineage and over-represents the decision-theory branch. Empty `evidence` field uniform null across all 43 sampled hub-incident edges (master-plan §T2-E pre-listed; thirteenth session in a row confirming graph-wide). Parametric-only review per master-plan §"Empirical-fortification branch" routine-mode prohibition (load-bearing until T1-A through T1-D close at the closeout per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md)); medium-confidence + mutation-implying verdicts (E-5, E-11, E-16, E-17, E-25, N-1, N-3) get fortified at the closeout per master-plan §"Forward pointers to closeout" / [ADR 0059](adr/0059-audit-time-structural-reference-fetching.md). The file is candidate-findings-only per master-plan §"Anti-scope" — disposition is interactive at closeout, not in this routine target.

Node-verdict tally: 5 sound-high (no granularity-mismatches; all 5 hubs concept-level appropriate). Substantive-defect rate 7/59 = **11.9%** — in band with prior subdomains (S-0115 aesthetics 5.3%, S-0114 political 10%, S-0113 science 10.5%, S-0110 mind 10.8%, S-0109 metaphysics 14.3%, S-0108 ethics 16.7%, S-0112 language 21%, S-0116 service 22%); below the cross-bridge baseline (35.2% per AUDIT-CB at S-0104) and well below the within-session expansion trigger (60% mid-sample). The hub-centrality finding validates as defense-side: the graph's most-central nodes are NOT the principal locus of substantive defects (87% sound across the 54 incident edges; all 5 hub nodes sound-high), suggesting the per-subdomain defect rates concentrate in lower-degree edges and nodes rather than the structural backbone. **Three pattern-aggregation surfaces strengthened for the closeout**: (1) HISTORICAL_INFLUENCE PREDICATE-ACTIVATION continued strengthening — the master-plan §"Structural reopen pre-flag" 10+ ADR-warranting threshold was already cleared at S-0104 + S-0116; this fire extends coverage from cross-bridges (S-0104) and within-service edges (S-0116) to the cross-bridge-from-history-terminator-to-substantive-domain class (E-43 + E-53 — both HIGH-confidence with literal named-example sources), bringing the cumulative count to 16+ historical-not-pedagogical findings across S-0081 / S-0104 / S-0116 / S-0119; AUDIT-HT-2 may add further history-terminator-anchored cross-bridge findings (vienna_circle_logical_positivism is in HUB 6–10 scope per the auto_target task description); the closeout's predicate-activation memo has decisive evidence; (2) NEW cross-cluster genus-species-inversion shape clustering across E-14 + E-29 + E-54 (three REVERSED findings in this single fire, two cross-bridges and one within-cluster) — distinct from prior routine-block reversal patterns (S-0112 tools-vs-position, S-0114 question-vs-answer, S-0105 frameworks-vs-motivations, S-0108 position-vs-criterion, S-0110 argument-vs-position, S-0112 / S-0113 developmental-arc, S-0115 cross-cluster-theoretical-thread-ordering); the shape is "more-specific concept (or specific application) is taught before the broader genus (or broader methodological thesis) that contains or generalizes it"; closeout may propose a `cross_bridge_genus_species_direction_inverted` validator soft-warn in addition to the four pre-listed proposals at master-plan §"Audit-system-input proposals"; the new `cross_bridge_genus_species_direction_inverted` shape is recorded as a candidate observation. ### Added (S-0118 — fix Issues #56, #57, #58)

- **[`engine/adr/0060-routine-wedge-detect-and-pause.md`](adr/0060-routine-wedge-detect-and-pause.md)** — new ADR introducing routine boot step 0c (between concurrency-lock acquire per ADR 0052 and target precondition per step 1). Closes the systemic gap that produced the S-0117 wedge (Issue #58): future halted-routine wedges are detected and idempotently produce ONE Issue + ONE HANDOFF entry instead of HANDOFF spam every hour. The auto-administrative-close alternative was rejected because synthesizing structured archive fields (outcome_summary / outcome_summary_soft_warns / mempalace_activity / next_session_handle / mode) without the halted session's input silently corrupts downstream telemetry per [ADR 0042](adr/0042-soft-warn-lifecycle-archive-canon.md) + [ADR 0049](adr/0049-scope-lock-at-boot-and-descope-reorder-audit-at-shutdown.md) + [ADR 0056](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md). Detect-and-pause stays read-only on shared state apart from idempotent HANDOFF + Issue authoring.
- **[`engine/tools/routine_wedge_detect.py`](tools/routine_wedge_detect.py)** — wedge-detection tool implementing the ADR 0060 mechanism. Inspects shared state (register_state.json, current.json, auto_target.json, HEAD-vs-origin/main) for the 6-conjunct wedge predicate; on detection idempotently authors a single GitHub Issue + a single HANDOFF.md section, commits, pushes via subprocess-bypass per ADR 0054 pattern. Exit codes 0 (no wedge) / 2 (wedge handled) / 3 (ambiguous shape) / 5 (generic failure). Idempotency short-circuit: if the HANDOFF section already exists for the wedged session_id, returns exit 2 immediately without re-authoring.
- **[`engine/tools/test_routine_wedge_detect.py`](tools/test_routine_wedge_detect.py)** — 14 pytests against tmp-dir bare-repo + clone fixtures covering each predicate conjunct's accept/reject path, idempotency (no double-author on re-invocation), `--dry-run` no-mutate, and `--skip-gh` HANDOFF-only mode.
- **[`engine/build_readiness/routine_wedge_detect_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/routine_wedge_detect_first_exercise.md)** — first-exercise readiness note per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md). T1-A (first natural production wedge) closes when the next halted-routine wedge naturally occurs.
- **[`engine/tools/probe_session_dir.py`](tools/probe_session_dir.py)** — boot-time probe modeled on `probe_repo.py` that scans the parent repo's engine/session/ for filenames matching the canonical macOS Finder / iCloud-sync conflict pattern (`current N.json` with literal space + digit). Closes Issue #57 (the S-0116 stray-file trip that blocked routine_lifecycle_push.py eager-claim). Wired into `validate.py --health-probe-only` alongside `probe_palace.py` and `probe_repo.py` so the existing LOUD attention surface in session-start.sh fires at boot if a stray file appears.
- **[`engine/tools/test_probe_session_dir.py`](tools/test_probe_session_dir.py)** — 6 pytests covering healthy / single stray / multiple strays sorted / archive subdir not flagged / unrelated filenames not flagged / not-in-a-repo no-op.
- **[`engine/tools/test_pre_commit_archive_filter.py`](tools/test_pre_commit_archive_filter.py)** — 4 regression tests for Issue #56 covering the filter-logic delta between `--diff-filter=A` (pre-fix, silently skipped git-mv renames) and `--diff-filter=AR` (post-fix, catches both close shapes).

### Added (S-0111 — routine session against T-PHASE-5-AUDIT task AUDIT-LOG — logic (philosophical) subdomain evidence file)

- **[`engine/build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit_evidence/logic.md`](build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit_evidence/logic.md)** — sixth evidence file for T-PHASE-5-AUDIT, authored by S-0111 (the sixth routine session post-S-0107 master-plan tightening). 12 of 34 within-logic edges (35.3% density) reviewed via deterministic md5(seed='AUDIT-LOG' || source_id || '|' || target_id) sampling across the single-file `0090_seed_logic_part1.sql` (P5-03 single-task seed covering the propositional/predicate/classical foundation tier + modal logic + conditionals + semantic paradox + vagueness + paraconsistent + deontic clusters) under the master-plan §"Per-edge prompt template" (verbatim — fixed per master-plan T1-A). 8 edge-anchored nodes (drawn from a 15-element edge-anchored union via deterministic md5(seed='AUDIT-LOG' || node_id) ordering) reviewed under the master-plan §"Per-node prompt template" (verbatim — fixed per master-plan T1-B). Edge-verdict tally: 11 sound + 1 defensible (E-7 conditional_logic→chisholm_paradox — multi-prereq overdetermined; deontic_logic→chisholm_paradox is also a seed edge at E-11 in this sample, the bare paradox derives from SDL apparatus + the classical material conditional + the deduction theorem, conditional_logic illuminates the response literature — Hansson 1969 dyadic deontic, Belnap-Horty stit, dropping contraction in relevance/linear logic — but is not strictly required for the basic Chisholm formulation; closeout disposition: retire OR retain as illuminating-the-response-literature with no graph mutation). Node-verdict tally: 8 sound, 0 granularity-mismatch, 0 authenticity concerns. Substantive-defect rate 1/20 = **5%** — LOWEST within-subdomain rate of the routine block to date; below S-0105 epistemology (5.4%), well below S-0108 ethics (16.7%), S-0109 metaphysics (14.3%), S-0110 mind (10.8%); well below the cross-bridge baseline (35.2% per AUDIT-CB at S-0104). The pattern fits the structural prediction that within-subdomain edges run cleaner than cross-domain bridges — and within-logic specifically runs cleanest because the formal-systems hierarchy (propositional ⊂ predicate ⊂ classical; modal as a propositional extension; deontic as a modal extension; conditionals as a propositional / modal question) tightly determines pedagogical direction in a way that contested philosophical concepts (e.g., the property-dualism / knowledge-argument relation in the mind seed) do not. Mid-sample expansion trigger nowhere near firing (half-sample defect 0/6 = 0%); standard 35% density held. Zero direction reversals (distinct from S-0110 mind 2 reversals; S-0108 ethics 1; S-0105 epistemology 1) — formal-systems subdomain has objectively right pedagogical directions in a way position-vs-argument subdomains do not. Zero granularity-mismatch verdicts (distinct from S-0105 N-8, S-0108 N-4 + N-9, S-0109 N-4 + N-6, S-0110 N-2) — foundation-level formal-system nodes (predicate_logic, classical_logic) at appropriate granularity, not discipline labels in the per-node prompt's warning sense. **One load-bearing aggregate observation surfaced for the closeout**: E-7 conditional_logic→chisholm_paradox is a NEW class of overdetermined edge — multi-prereq edge where the bare paradox is derivable from a more proximate prereq (deontic_logic) and the second prereq (conditional_logic) illuminates the response literature but isn't strictly required for the basic formulation; distinct in shape from the species-shadowing-genus pattern S-0108 E-17/E-20, the long-distance shortcut pattern S-0109 E-10, the tools-vs-topic ordering pattern S-0110 E-12 — same redundancy-class umbrella but a new sub-shape. **Did NOT corroborate S-0110 argument-vs-position directionality candidate** — logic subdomain's node taxonomy has no "arguments" vs "positions" analogue. Parametric-only review per master-plan §"Empirical-fortification branch" routine-mode prohibition (load-bearing until T1-A through T1-D close at the closeout per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md)); medium-confidence + mutation-implying verdicts (E-7) get fortified at the closeout per master-plan §"Forward pointers to closeout" / [ADR 0059](adr/0059-audit-time-structural-reference-fetching.md). The file is candidate-findings-only per master-plan §"Anti-scope" — disposition is interactive at closeout, not in this routine target.

### Added (S-0106 — interactive build session: ADR 0059 + fetch_structural_reference.py + Phase 5 audit methodology + Tier 4 fetch-policy)

- **[ADR 0059](adr/0059-audit-time-structural-reference-fetching.md)** — engine ADR authorizing audit-time fetching of public Tier 4 structural references (SEP / IEP / Wikipedia) for verdict fortification, under four union-sufficient conditions: (1) S-0103 source-identity anonymization mandatory on URL-fetched briefs; (2) bounded ephemeral lifecycle (`tempfile.TemporaryDirectory` purged on context exit; no on-disk cache; no cross-session persistence); (3) polite-fetcher discipline (declared User-Agent identifying the project, robots.txt via `urllib.robotparser`, per-host rate-limit default 2.0s, bounded fetch budget default 20); (4) per-source policy in `product/docs/content-strategy.md` Tier 4 (SEP / IEP / Wikipedia: fetchable; Routledge / Oxford Reference: out of scope, paywalled). Authoring-time posture under [ADR 0046](../product/adr/0046-structural-reference-posture-extends-to-philosophy-reference-works.md) is unchanged; [ADR 0011](../product/adr/0011-no-hosted-copyrighted-material.md) ceiling is unchanged; [ADR 0057](adr/0057-adversarial-stance-for-health-check-audits.md) "fresh content probe at audit-time" posture is operationalized for graph audits. Failure-mode discrimination via exit codes 0/2/3/4/5/6 matches the [`routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py) / [`apply_migration.py`](tools/apply_migration.py) wrapper pattern. Standing-capability fetcher and per-source ADR for paywalled members of the [ADR 0046](../product/adr/0046-structural-reference-posture-extends-to-philosophy-reference-works.md) class are explicit deferred-future-ADRs (named, not hedged). [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) trigger-criterion evaluation lands in Consequences: strict trigger does not fire (1 ops doc + 2 tooling files + 4 doc amendments under threshold); voluntary first-exercise readiness note authored at [`engine/build_readiness/fetch_structural_reference_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/fetch_structural_reference_first_exercise.md) per the gate's "trigger when in doubt" bias. Adjudicates the user's S-0106 question on parametric-only stance per the Option A carve-out at `~/.claude/plans/i-want-an-adversarial-toasty-storm.md`.
- **[`engine/tools/fetch_structural_reference.py`](tools/fetch_structural_reference.py)** — paired URL-input counterpart to [`engine/tools/parse_structural_reference.py`](tools/parse_structural_reference.py). The new tool composes the existing parser via its public API (`select_adapter` + `extract` + `extract_entries` + `emit_focusing_brief` + `serialize_brief`); the parser's anti-fetch contract is preserved verbatim — `parse_structural_reference.py` is unchanged. The S-0103 anonymization helpers (`is_publication_name_shaped`, `strip_publication_name_suffix`, the `serialize_brief()` post-filter) are reused via direct function import — no fork, no reimplementation. `FetchSession` context manager wraps `tempfile.TemporaryDirectory` + per-host rate-limit + fetch budget + robots.txt cache; on context exit the tmpdir is purged and all cache state is dropped. `fetch_and_parse(url, document_type, session=session)` is the high-level entry; CLI mode (`python3 engine/tools/fetch_structural_reference.py --url ... --document-type encyclopedia`) is also exposed. Recursive-walk anonymization invariant `_assert_anonymized()` catches publication-name-shaped strings, raw URLs, and concatenated publisher patterns at any depth in the brief; violation raises `AnonymizationViolation` (exit code 6 — load-bearing; the brief MUST NOT reach the LLM). `TIER_4_FETCHABLE_HOSTS` constant is a sanity backstop on the [`product/docs/content-strategy.md`](../product/docs/content-strategy.md) policy table.
- **[`engine/tools/test_fetch_structural_reference.py`](tools/test_fetch_structural_reference.py)** — 27 tests covering `TestFetchSessionLifecycle` (tmpdir purge, parameter validation, max-fetches budget enforcement); `TestRobotsTxtCompliance` (allow / disallow / unavailable / 404); `TestRateLimit` (first fetch immediate, second fetch sleeps the deficit asserted within 0.05s); `TestNetworkFailureAndRetry` (transient → succeed; persistent → exit 4); `TestAnonymizationInvariant` (clean passes; publication-name at top / nested / deeply-nested raises; URL raises; concatenated pattern raises) — adversarial fixtures use synthetic-publisher tokens `Acme`, `FakeReference`, `MockPublisher`, `GenericSource` per the S-0103 implementation discipline; `TestComposition` (synthetic SEP-shaped HTML round-trips through the parser via the fetch path and produces `FocusingBrief` with entries; unknown document_type raises with exit code 5); `TestExitCodes` (CLI mode emits codes 0/2/3/4/6 via `main(...)` invocation against synthetic stubs); `TestTier4Hosts` (sanity backstop on the policy constant). All 27 pass at S-0106; existing 155 [`engine/tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py`](tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py) tests still pass.
- **[`engine/build_readiness/fetch_structural_reference_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/fetch_structural_reference_first_exercise.md)** — voluntary mechanism-first-exercise gate report per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md). Six T1 findings recorded: T1-A through T1-D pending the first interactive exercise (anonymization invariant against real SEP fetch; robots.txt parse against real host; rate-limit observed against real network; one-fetch round-trip yields non-empty entries); T1-E and T1-F resolved at S-0106 (User-Agent declaration; failure-mode discrimination via exit codes 0/2/3/4/5/6). Three T2 findings documented (per-host rate-limit may be insufficient under heavy session pace; anonymization regex correctness depends on structural-pattern coverage; CLI's `--max-fetches` budget is per-invocation not per-session). Three T3 deferred forward-pointers (standing-capability ADR; per-source acquisition ADR for paywalled members; `fetch_budget_exceeded_session` validator soft-warn). T1-A through T1-D close at the first interactive audit-closeout session that fortifies S-0104 medium-confidence verdicts.

### Changed (S-0106 — ADR 0047 + Phase 5 audit methodology + content-strategy.md + cross-references + STATE.md + register_state)

- **[ADR 0047](adr/0047-structural-reference-parser-tool-and-adversarial-triage-workflow.md) Consequences amended in-place** with a paired URL-input tool back-pointer per [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) amendment asymmetry. The amendment notes the scope-clean separation: `parse_structural_reference.py` remains file-input only with its anti-fetch non-responsibility preserved verbatim; `fetch_structural_reference.py` is URL-input only and composes the parser's public API after a polite-fetcher wrapper. The S-0103 source-identity anonymization mechanism is shared via direct function reuse. The "Open future ADRs" clause's per-source acquisition pointer is the conceptual ancestor of [ADR 0059](adr/0059-audit-time-structural-reference-fetching.md), but [ADR 0059](adr/0059-audit-time-structural-reference-fetching.md) covers the *public* Tier 4 case — paywalled per-source ADRs remain deferred.
- **[`engine/build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit.md`](build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit.md) methodology amended in-place** with a new "Optional empirical-fortification branch (added at S-0106 per ADR 0059)" subsection between the per-edge / per-node prompt templates and the evidence file schema. Routine sessions invoke the branch ONLY for medium-confidence verdicts that imply a graph mutation (reversal, retyping, removal, granularity-mismatch). High-confidence parametric verdicts skip the branch — the marginal cost of fetching does not justify the additional confidence gain. The procedure documents the per-verdict shape (identify canonical Tier 4 URL → invoke `fetch_and_parse()` within an audit-session `FetchSession` → compare structural framing → update confidence OR change verdict, recording both for closeout adjudication). Pre-S-0106 evidence files (S-0104 cross-bridges, S-0105 epistemology) remain valid as parametric-only baselines; the closeout may revisit specific medium-confidence verdicts using this branch if the user judges the cost-benefit favorable.
- **[`product/docs/content-strategy.md`](../product/docs/content-strategy.md) Tier 4 amended in-place** with a new "Audit-time fetch-policy (added at S-0106 per ADR 0059)" subsection. Per-host policy table authorizes plato.stanford.edu, iep.utm.edu, and en.wikipedia.org for audit-time fetching with polite-fetcher discipline; explicitly excludes rep.routledge.com and oxfordreference.com (paywalled — institutional-credential fetching requires a per-source ADR, not authored at S-0106). The `TIER_4_FETCHABLE_HOSTS` constant in the new tool is a sanity backstop on the policy; modifications to either side require modifications to both in the same commit.
- **[`engine/operations/cross-references.md`](operations/cross-references.md)** — new ADR 0059 row mapping it to its consumers (the new tool, its tests, the master-plan methodology amendment, the build-readiness first-exercise note, the content-strategy.md fetch-policy table, and the ADR 0047 Consequences amendment).

### Added (S-0103 — cleanup-batch session: combined Issues #48 + #49 — parse_structural_reference.py source-identity anonymization + body-font-entry/page-header-runner detector tier)

- **Module-scope structural source-identity anonymization primitives** in [`engine/tools/parse_structural_reference.py`](tools/parse_structural_reference.py): `PUBLICATION_NAME_PATTERN` (whole-form regex matching `<X> Encyclopedia/Dictionary/Companion/Handbook/Reference/Compendium of/to <Y>`), `PUBLICATION_NAME_PATTERN_CONCATENATED` (sibling for sources that strip whitespace from page-header runners), `PUBLICATION_NAME_SUFFIX_STRIPPER` (structural suffix stripper subsuming the previously-enumerated SEP/IEP per-publisher patterns). Two helpers: `is_publication_name_shaped(text)` and `strip_publication_name_suffix(title)`. The structural alternation tokens (Encyclopedia / Dictionary / Companion / Handbook / Reference / Compendium) are reference-work-type descriptors, not source-identity tokens — preserving the [ADR 0047](adr/0047-structural-reference-parser-tool-and-adversarial-triage-workflow.md) decision 4 parametric-knowledge boundary at the project's own config layer. Closes [Issue #49](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/49).
- **`PDFInputAdapter._emit_page_header_headings()` third-tier heading detector** for the structural class characterized by body-font entries with page-header runners as the only entry indicator. Source-agnostic per ADR 0047 decision 1. Gated by `outline_count >= 50` (mirrors existing font-size detector short-circuit). Per page: extracts first-line runner; skips publication-name-shaped lines (anonymization filter — runners commonly carry the publication name on alternating pages per standard typography); tests page-header-shape predicate (`_is_page_header_shaped`: short, capitalized, no terminal punctuation, distinct from body); splits on whitespace, falling through to `_split_camel_concat()` (case-transition boundaries) for sources that strip whitespace; re-applies the anonymization filter per-token after splitting; emits surviving tokens as level-1 heading elements. Wired into `extract()` orchestration after `_emit_font_size_headings()` so the multi-fallback ladder is now outline → font-size → page-header. Closes [Issue #48](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/48).
- **Defense-in-depth partition-layer filter** in `extract_entries()` — partitions whose first heading text matches `is_publication_name_shaped()` are dropped before becoming `Entry` records. Catches publication-name leakage from any emit path (outline, font-size, page-header, text-pattern), not only the new third-tier detector. Pairs with the emit-time filter in `_emit_page_header_headings()` and the title-detection filter in `detect_title()` for layered protection.
- **Test coverage**: `TestSerializeBriefAnonymization` (5 tests in [`engine/tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py`](tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py)), `TestPublicationNamePattern` (10 tests + parametrize expansions to 32 variants), `TestPageHeaderEntryIndicator` (12 tests), `TestPageHeaderAnonymizationInvariant` (6 tests including the recursive brief-walk anti-leak gate and the alternating-runner adversarial fixture). All test data uses synthetic publisher tokens (Acme, FakeReference, MockPublisher, GenericSource, PlaceholderName) per the source-identity-in-mechanism-corpus discipline.

### Fixed (S-0103 — `serialize_brief()` source-identity anonymization at the serialization boundary)

- **`serialize_brief()` in [`engine/tools/parse_structural_reference.py`](tools/parse_structural_reference.py)** strips `source_path` (top-level) and `source_url` (per-entry) from the JSON output via a `dataclasses.asdict()` post-filter. The in-memory `FocusingBrief` and `Entry` dataclasses retain the fields because internal consumers (notably `detect_entry_id` slug derivation) still need them; the strip happens only on the dict copy. Module docstring "Output schema" block updated to remove the stripped fields and add an anonymization-rationale note cross-referencing ADR 0047 decision 4.
- **`detect_title()`** rewired to call `strip_publication_name_suffix()` on the candidate, then test the stripped result against `is_publication_name_shaped()` — whole-shape matches return None and the H1 fallback chain triggers. The H1 fallback also skips publication-name-shaped headings. `document_type_config` is preserved in the signature for interface compatibility but no longer consulted (the structural stripper subsumes the previous config lookup).
- Both fixes close [Issue #49](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/49) — `FocusingBrief` JSON no longer leaks publisher identity to the downstream adversarial-triage LLM.
