- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) — **fix-in-context.** `_check_validate_passes` was treating validate.py exit 1 as fail; per `auto_target.schema.md` (validate_passes section), criterion passes iff zero hard-fails. validate.py main() exits 1 whenever any soft-warn fires; the persistent `issue_collision` soft-warns from open Issues #1/#2/#3/#4 keyword-matching every routine session would have blocked all routine `validate_passes` criteria. Fixed: criterion now passes when validate.py exits 0 OR 1; only exit 2 (hard fails) is fail. Updated docstring explains the three-exit-code semantic.
- [`engine/tools/test_check_target.py`](tools/test_check_target.py) — **3 new regression tests** for the validate_passes exit-code behavior: `test_validate_passes_exit_zero_passes`, `test_validate_passes_exit_one_passes`, `test_validate_passes_exit_two_fails`. All three exercise `_check_validate_passes` against monkeypatched `subprocess.run` with the three documented validate.py exit codes. Suite rises 30 → 33 tests for check_target; full pytest suite 516 → 519.


- [`engine/adr/0051-routine-mode-and-engine-loop.md`](adr/0051-routine-mode-and-engine-loop.md) — **new engine ADR.** Third session mode alongside exploration and build: unattended cadence-driven Claude Code Routines that read `engine/session/auto_target.json`, pick the next eligible task, run plan-then-scope-check, execute or exit gracefully without claiming. Two-layer architecture: master plan session (interactive, `/start-engine`) authors the target contract; engine loop (unattended, `/start-routine`) executes it. They share only the eager-claim ritual; everything else (boot procedure, scope rules, commit posture, permission model, shutdown logic) is mode-specific. Six-layer defense in depth: boot-time scope-check on the session plan, commit-time scope-check on staged files (task `scope_lock` ∪ operational allowlist), master-plan integrity hard-fail on non-status diffs to `auto_target.json`, existing `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`, new `routine_issue_spam` soft-warn at >3 issues per session, new `routine_no_target_reference` soft-warn for plan-target alignment. **Paperclip rejected** (Anthropic April-2026 third-party-orchestration policy excludes from subscription coverage; Paperclip GitHub #1163 and #3270 confirm `claude_local` adapter's subscription path is incompatible with unattended dispatch). Reasoning preserved in ADR 0051 Alternatives Considered. Phase 5 epistemology build-readiness gate (twice-displaced) reframed: the gate report at `engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md` is now authored by the Phase 5 master plan session (S-0045+) as part of producing the `auto_target.json` contract.
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) — **new Layer 1 ops doc** (reference-shaped per ADR 0044). Target file schema, master plan session procedure, routine boot procedure, criterion catalog, scope-lock model, mixing interactive and routine sessions, troubleshooting.
- [`engine/session/auto_target.schema.md`](session/auto_target.schema.md) — **new schema reference doc.** Top-level fields (`target_id`, `goal`, `paused`, `max_sessions`, `max_wall_clock_hours`, `tasks`); per-task fields (`id`, `name`, `depends_on`, `criteria`, `scope_lock`, `status`, `blocked_reason`); five criterion types (`migration_applied`, `validate_passes`, `adr_status`, `file_exists`, `predicate`) with shape examples; complete Phase 5 sketch example.
- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) — **new tool.** Predicate runner for target file criteria. Five criterion types ship at landing; predicate-registry escape hatch for non-standard criteria. CLI: `--target`, `--task-id`, `--json`. 30 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/check_routine_scope.py`](tools/check_routine_scope.py) — **new tool.** Three enforcement points: plan-vs-scope (boot-time, `--plan`), staged-vs-scope (commit-time, `--staged`), master-plan integrity (commit-time, automatic when `auto_target.json` is staged). Segment-aware glob matching (`*` segment-bounded, `**` cross-segment). Operational allowlist constants. CLI: `--plan PATH`, `--staged`, `--task-id`, `--target`, `--repo-root`. 40 unit tests.
- [`.claude/commands/start-routine.md`](../.claude/commands/start-routine.md) — **new slash command.** Architecturally distinct from `/start-engine` per S-0044 user direction: bolting routine-mode into `/start-engine` conflated five differences (boot, scope, commit, permission, shutdown). Two clean entry points share only the eager-claim ritual.
- [`.claude/skills/routine-mode-lifecycle/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/routine-mode-lifecycle/SKILL.md) — **new recipe-shaped Skill** (per ADR 0044). Mirrors the routine boot procedure in routine-mode-operations.md. `disable-model-invocation: true` — invoked deliberately, not auto-fired.
- 3 new test files: `test_check_target.py` (30 tests), `test_check_routine_scope.py` (40 tests), `test_validate_routine_mode.py` (12 tests). 82 new tests total. Full suite 516 passing.
- **GitHub Issue #3 filed** per ADR 0048 issue-discipline: `/start-engine` boot procedure should detect `current_status: in_progress` with a recent `started_at` and refuse to claim mid-routine. Out of S-0044 scope (would expand the session beyond declared scope per ADR 0049); routed to Issue. Surfaced when user asked "What if I start a manual interactive session while routine mode sessions are running?" — apparatus assumes one active session at a time and would corrupt state on collision. Procedural workaround documented in routine-mode-operations.md "Mixing interactive and routine sessions" (set `paused: true`, wait for in-flight to close, then start interactive).

### Changed (S-0044 — Routine-mode foundation)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **new `validate_routine_mode()` function** with two soft-warn categories: `routine_no_target_reference` (current_plan.md exists but doesn't mention active task's id or name; suggests routine session drifted from target) and `routine_issue_spam` (>3 GitHub issues created since session's `started_at`; defense-in-depth against confused-session containment; legitimate fix-this-many findings ride through). Both no-op when not in routine-mode. Wired into default-mode dispatch. Default-mode validator check count rises 21 → 23.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) — **new routine-mode scope-check section.** Always-invoked when `engine/session/auto_target.json` exists; the tool itself detects routine-mode (target + current_plan.md + in_progress task) and exits 0 silently when not applicable. Hard-fails staged out-of-scope paths AND non-status diffs to `auto_target.json` from routine commits.
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — **routine-mode reframed as a separate lifecycle**, not a branch of /start-engine's boot procedure. Notes /start-routine + routine-mode-lifecycle Skill as the architecturally distinct path. They share only the eager-claim ritual.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **third session mode** (`routine`) added alongside exploration and build, with explicit posture for scope_lock invariance, operational allowlist, `gh issue create` authorization, HANDOFF additions, and master-plan-revision-via-HANDOFF rule. Mechanization-list bullet added for ADR 0051 routine-mode scope-lock and master-plan integrity. Topical pointer added for routine-mode-operations.md. Note about four-skills now (with `routine-mode-lifecycle` joining the existing three).
- [`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md) — **Paperclip integration entry rewritten** as "Rejected at S-0044, superseded by ADR 0051" with the cost-calculus rationale and the conditions under which Paperclip becomes a reasonable revisit.
- [`engine/operations/README.md`](operations/README.md) — `routine-mode-operations.md` added to Session protocol section.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — index extended with ADR 0051; engine ADR count rises 16 → 17 (corrected count line that had drifted to 15 pre-S-0044); project total 50 → 51.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) (lines 1905-1906) — **pre-existing unused `# type: ignore` paired** for psycopg imports as `# type: ignore[import-not-found,unused-ignore]`. Mid-session fix-in-context per CLAUDE.md — paired form satisfies both the pre-commit hook's mypy invocation (which can't see venv-installed psycopg in some subprocess contexts) and standalone post-cache-clear mypy (which can). Pre-existing tech debt that mypy cache had been masking at S-0043 close.

### Added (S-0043 — Project venv with hook PATH wiring; mempalace migration; tiktoken activation)
- [`engine/adr/0050-project-venv-and-hook-path-wiring.md`](adr/0050-project-venv-and-hook-path-wiring.md) — **new engine ADR.** Project-local Python venv at `<main_repo>/.venv/`, managed by `uv`, pinned to Python 3.12 via tracked `.python-version`. Hook scripts resolve `python3` and other tool entry points via a sourcing-time PATH prepend in `engine/tools/scrub_env.sh` — worktree-local `.venv/` preferred, main repo's `.venv/` fallback. Single intervention point: PATH preservation across `scrubbed_env()` (per ADR 0045) propagates through every nested invocation, so `validate.py` and all eight current Python invocation sites pick up venv tools without per-script edits. Three previously implicit deps now explicitly pinned in `engine/tools/requirements.txt`: `chromadb` (was carried only by user-scope incidental install), `tiktoken` (activates the accurate-tokenizer branch in `scan_context_telemetry.py` per ADR 0049), `mempalace` (migrated from user-scope system Python 3.9 → project venv 3.12, addressing recurring Python-version issues with the tool). MemPalace upgrade 3.3.3 → 3.3.4 verified at S-0043 against Issues #1 and #2: Issue #1 reproduces verbatim (wing-filtered search "Internal error"); Issue #2 wing-derivation behavior changed (`wing_<last-token>` instead of full encoded path) but per-worktree fragmentation persists and the new `wing_paideia` is distinct from the documented bare `paideia` wing.
- [`.python-version`](../.python-version) — **new tracked file** at main repo root. Pins Python to `3.12`. uv reads this when creating venvs.

### Changed (S-0043 — Project venv migration)
- [`engine/tools/scrub_env.sh`](tools/scrub_env.sh) — **adds sourcing-time PATH-prepend behavior** alongside the existing `scrub_git_env` function. Resolves worktree root and main-repo root via `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` and `git rev-parse --git-common-dir` (with `realpath` normalization for the relative-path return case); prefers worktree-local `.venv/bin/`, falls back to main repo's; idempotent via `case ":$PATH:"` substring guard; silent no-op when neither venv exists or when sourced outside a git repo. Header comment expanded to document both responsibilities (scrub + wire) and motivating failures (S-0033 GIT_DIR leak; S-0043 system-Python coupling).
- [`engine/tools/requirements.txt`](tools/requirements.txt) — **three new explicit pins.** `chromadb>=0.5.0` (closes silent-dependency gap; previously imported by `probe_palace.py` but not declared). `tiktoken>=0.7.0` (activates `tiktoken-o200k_base` tokenizer in `scan_context_telemetry.py` per ADR 0049; archives going forward carry accurate token counts rather than `chars-div-4-fallback`). `mempalace>=3.3.3` (migrates mempalace from user-scope into project venv per ADR 0050 decision).
- [`.mcp.json`](../.mcp.json) — **mempalace-mcp command path updated** to `<main_repo>/.venv/bin/mempalace-mcp`. Local-only edit (file is gitignored). Hook wrapper at `engine/tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh` resolves mempalace via PATH (now venv-prepended) and needs no edits.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) — **Known issues section updated for 3.3.4 verification.** Issue #1 entry adds re-verification note (bug reproduces verbatim in 3.3.4). Issue #2 entry rewritten to describe the 3.3.4 `_wing_from_transcript_path` `rsplit("-", 1)[-1]` behavior change and the new `wing_paideia` vs. bare `paideia` wing distinction.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — index extended with ADR 0050; engine ADR count rises 15 → 16; project total 49 → 50.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — mechanization-list bullet added for project venv + ADR 0050.
- [`engine/session/current.json`](session/current.json) — S-0043's own `current.json` written at eager-claim with `declared_scope` (including `phase: NA-engine-apparatus` operational marker) per ADR 0049.

### Added (S-0042 — Engine apparatus improvements: HANDOFF/Issues split + multi-axis health-check + scope-lock + telemetry)
- [`engine/adr/0048-handoff-narrowing-and-github-issues-for-cross-session-deferrals.md`](adr/0048-handoff-narrowing-and-github-issues-for-cross-session-deferrals.md) — **new engine ADR.** Narrows HANDOFF.md to session-internal handoffs (partial-closure, in-flight recovery, atomic ownership transfer); routes cross-session deferrals to GitHub Issues with a six-label taxonomy (`bug`, `enhancement`, `tech-debt`, `cleanup`, `health-check-finding`, `upstream`) plus one priority label (`priority:urgent`). Boot-time backlog visibility via `scan_issue_backlog.py` + `session-start.sh` integration; scope-collision detection via `scan_issue_collisions.py` + `validate.py` integration. Closes the cleanup-treadmill failure mode the planning thread named: every HANDOFF entry creates implicit "next session must address this" pressure; Issues sit silently in a labelled backlog with cleanup-batch workflow.
- [`engine/adr/0049-scope-lock-at-boot-and-descope-reorder-audit-at-shutdown.md`](adr/0049-scope-lock-at-boot-and-descope-reorder-audit-at-shutdown.md) — **new engine ADR.** Three coupled mechanisms: (1) `declared_scope` field at boot in `current.json`; (2) scope-delivery audit at shutdown with structured `{delivered, user_confirmed_changes, explanation}` field; (3) session-end context telemetry via transcript tokenization (closes the context-state opacity failure mode — Claude Code does not expose context usage to running code, but the transcript JSONL is the available proxy). Three new validator soft-warns: `empty_declared_scope`, `phase_mismatch_declared_scope`, `scope_delivery_non_yes`. Multi-session scope-erosion signal at next boot. Build-readiness gate gains a no-descoping-or-reordering clause closing the S-0037 phase-5-before-4.5 vector.
- [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) — **new Layer 1 ops doc.** HANDOFF-vs-Issue decision rule (immediacy + ownership + session-context-dependency criteria); label taxonomy with semantic definitions; Issue body shape requiring an "Affected files" section that the collision-detection scanner consumes; cleanup-batch workflow; boot-time visibility surfaces; scope-collision detection wiring.
- [`engine/build_readiness/engine_apparatus_improvements_s0042.md`](build_readiness/engine_apparatus_improvements_s0042.md) — **new build-readiness gate report.** Compressed gate execution per ADR 0040 (planning thread carried steps 1-5 conversationally with 3 parallel Explore agents + user-directed Tier 1 resolution on the orphan-definition lens correction). Cold-review pass against citations applied four sharpenings (test count made dynamic; T2-A regex aligned with existing pattern style; T2-F phase example clarified; T2-G ambiguity resolved with structured field shape).
- [`engine/tools/scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/scan_issue_backlog.py) — **new tool.** Wraps `gh issue list`, counts by canonical label set, surfaces FYI line at every boot or LOUD attention block when `priority:urgent` count > 0. Best-effort: `gh` failure → stderr note + exit 0. 16 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/scan_issue_collisions.py`](tools/scan_issue_collisions.py) — **new tool.** Reads `current.json`'s `declared_scope` (with `working_on` fallback for pre-ADR-0049 sessions), tokenizes for keywords (lowercase, drop stopwords + short tokens), collects staged-files paths, queries open Issues, soft-warns per match. Word-boundary matching avoids spurious hits. 25 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/scan_orphans.py`](tools/scan_orphans.py) — **new tool.** Five-axis multi-dimensional dead-weight scanner: reference-count (<3 inbound refs), last-mod-age (only 1 substantive commit AND inbound-refs below 5-ref ceiling), register-emptiness (markdown table headers with no data rows), ops-doc-uncited (engine/operations/*.md with 0 archive citations in last 20 sessions), stale-pending-marker (decide-trigger / decide-before / open decide-by markers in low-commit-count files). Output: per-candidate annotated markdown for the audit's "is this file doing the work it was created to do?" triage. Verified on live repo: surfaces `ideation.md` (register-empty), `sub-agent-validation.md` and `tools-sweep-worktrees.md` (multi-axis), `prep-paideia-prompt-pack.md` (stale-marker). 18 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/scan_context_telemetry.py`](tools/scan_context_telemetry.py) — **new tool.** Auto-detects session transcript at `~/.claude/projects/<encoded-project-path>/<session-id>.jsonl` (most-recently-modified .jsonl), tokenizes with tiktoken `o200k_base` when installed (chars/4 fallback otherwise), writes `transcript_token_estimate` + `transcript_token_pct` + `tokenizer_used` to `current.json` for the cross-session "running too long / too short / high variance" judgment in the rewritten health-check Session-load trend section. 14 unit tests.
- **GitHub Issues #1 + #2 filed** as the seed `bug + upstream` exercise of the new tracker per ADR 0048: [#1](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/1) wing-filtered search throws Internal error, [#2](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/2) hook auto-capture creates one wing per worktree. Both upstream in mempalace 3.3.3 (not in-project remediable). Documentation cross-references the S-0040 HANDOFF entries (Resolved) and the workaround at `engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`.
- 7 GitHub label definitions confirmed in the repo: `bug`, `enhancement`, `tech-debt`, `cleanup`, `health-check-finding`, `upstream`, `priority:urgent` per ADR 0048 taxonomy.
- 6 new test files: `test_scan_issue_backlog.py` (16 tests), `test_scan_issue_collisions.py` (25 tests), `test_scan_orphans.py` (18 tests), `test_scan_context_telemetry.py` (14 tests), `test_validate_scope_discipline.py` (14 tests), `test_validate_issue_collisions.py` (4 tests). 91 new tests total. Full suite 434 passing; ruff + mypy --strict clean.

### Changed (S-0042 — Engine apparatus improvements)
- [`engine/tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py`](tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py) — **fifth disposition pattern added** to `_VALID_DISPOSITION_PATTERNS`: `re.compile(r"^tracked-as-issue\s+#\d+$")`. Hint message extended with the fifth bullet. Module docstring updated to describe the pattern's purpose (cross-session deferral routed to Issues per ADR 0048). 2 new tests covering accept/reject cases.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **two new validation functions.** `validate_issue_collisions()` wraps `scan_issue_collisions.py` (new `issue_collision` soft-warn category; best-effort posture; missing-scanner soft-warn). `validate_scope_discipline()` reads `current.json` and emits up to three soft-warns: `empty_declared_scope`, `phase_mismatch_declared_scope` (substring + heuristic-token match against `build_plan/MANIFEST.md`; `NA-` prefix opts out for operational sessions), `scope_delivery_non_yes` (warn fires regardless of `user_confirmed_changes`; the warn is signal for cross-session aggregation). Both functions wired into default-mode dispatch. Default-mode validator check count rises 17 → 21.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **two new boot surfaces.** Issues backlog visibility (between probe and persistent-warn surfaces): runs `scan_issue_backlog.py`, surfaces the FYI line at every boot. Multi-session scope-erosion signal (after persistent-warn surface): walks last 5 archives, counts `scope_delivery.delivered == false`, surfaces stderr block at 3-of-5 threshold. `log_ok` line gains `backlog=$BACKLOG_STATUS scope_non_yes=$SCOPE_NON_YES` telemetry fields.
- [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) — **rewritten audit section** around the operative diagnostic question ("Is this thing doing the work it was created to do, or is it plumbing waiting for a function that never arrived?") borrowed verbatim from the user's framing during the S-0042 planning thread. New "Mechanical inputs" section names `scan_orphans.py` as the per-candidate triage feeder. Required: at least one non-obvious finding not on any mechanical scanner's output (forces meta-analysis on top of mechanical surfaces). New "Infrastructure-without-function" posture sharpens the dead-weight category — each candidate ends with explicit disposition (retire / convert to active use / preserve with reason; "leave it for now" without naming why is itself the failure mode the audit exists to catch). Session-load trend section consumes the new ADR 0049 telemetry. Report template restructured to put the operative diagnostic + non-obvious finding sections first (the report is byproduct, not the deliverable).
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — **eager-claim ritual writes `declared_scope` and `scope_delivery: null`** in `current.json` template per ADR 0049. Validator soft-warns named.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **two new steps.** Step 7a (scope-delivery audit per ADR 0049): explicit literal prompt to the AI (`Did you deliver the declared scope? If no, why not? Did anything get descoped, reordered, or deferred mid-session — even with user confirmation?`) → structured field write to `current.json`. Step 7b (context telemetry per ADR 0049 cross-cutting addition): run `scan_context_telemetry.py` to capture transcript token estimate; fields travel with archive in step 9.
- [`engine/operations/build-readiness-gate.md`](operations/build-readiness-gate.md) — **new step 4a no-descoping-or-reordering clause** per ADR 0049. The gate session itself is a descoping vector — quietly trimming the chunk's deliverables or proposing reorderings ("Phase 5 before Phase 4.5") becomes the failure mode the scope-discipline machinery exists to catch. Any reduction OR reordering must be flagged to the user explicitly, not silently absorbed into the gate report.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) — **four new soft-warn category entries** documenting `issue_collision`, `empty_declared_scope`, `phase_mismatch_declared_scope`, `scope_delivery_non_yes`.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **"Default to fix-in-context" section updated** with the HANDOFF.md vs. GitHub Issues routing rule per ADR 0048 (`tracked-as-issue #<num>` is the fifth disposition form; cross-session deferrals default to Issues; HANDOFF.md narrows to session-internal handoffs).
- [`engine/operations/README.md`](operations/README.md) — `issue-discipline.md` added to Session protocol section.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — index extended with ADRs 0048, 0049; engine ADR count rises 13 → 15; project total 47 → 49.
- [`engine/session/current.json`](session/current.json) — S-0042's own `current.json` updated with `declared_scope` (including `phase: NA-engine-apparatus` operational marker) and `scope_delivery: null` placeholder.
- All three Skill mirrors updated per ADR 0044 doc → skill direction: `session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md` (declared_scope template), `session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md` (steps 7a + 7b), `build-readiness-gate/SKILL.md` (step 4a clause).

### Fixed (S-0041 — Cadence-trigger overdue-catchup logic + second project health check)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **strict-modulo cadence trigger replaced with overdue-catchup tracking.** The S-0031 strict-modulo logic (`next_id mod cadence == 0`) was correct at the natural-cadence slot but introduced a silent-slide failure mode: when the cadence-aligned slot was consumed by user-directed work that deferred the audit (S-0040's slot was claimed for the deferred MemPalace wing-filter fix per S-0040's outcome_summary), the trigger silently slid forward by a full cadence — the next firing would have landed at S-0050, a 19-session gap nearly 2x the configured cadence. The S-0041 boot caught the slide only because the user explicitly asked "this session is one past health check; why is it not engaging?" — discovery surface was AI-noticing-after-being-prompted, not mechanical-detection. New logic: read `last_audit_session` from `register_state.json`, compute `slots_since = next_id - last_audit_session`, fire when `slots_since >= cadence`. Two surfaces: "due" at the natural-cadence slot, "overdue" at every later slot until the audit fires. Legacy fallback: when `last_audit_session` is absent (legacy `register_state.json`), revert to strict-modulo with a `last-audit-absent-falling-back-to-strict-modulo` log line so the regression is visible. Telemetry log_ok lines now carry `cadence-fires`, `cadence-mode`, `slots-since` instead of `cadence-remainder`.
- [`engine/session/register_state.json`](session/register_state.json) — **schema gains `last_audit_session` field** (bootstrap value `S-0030`, the first audit) plus a `last_audit_session_field_history` array recording the field-addition rationale. The field is the canonical "audit happened" anchor that the SessionStart hook and validate.py's `health_check_overdue` check both consume.
- [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) — **`emit_report` bumps `register_state.json.last_audit_session`** to the report's session_id at non-dry-run report-emit time. New helper `bump_last_audit_session` performs the write with stderr-warning fallbacks (absent file, malformed JSON, write failure). Best-effort: failures do not poison the audit (the report is the durable artifact; the field bump is advisory tracking).
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **new `health_check_overdue` soft-warn category** added to `validate_repo_structure()`. Defense-in-depth so a silently-failing SessionStart hook (the S-0033 / S-0034 vector pattern) cannot mask the slide. Fires when `(register_state.json.next_id - last_audit_session) > cadence` (strictly past the natural firing slot — the natural slot is the hook's "due" surface, not an overdue condition). Skips quietly when `last_audit_session` is absent; the `checks_run` field still records the attempt. Default-mode validator check count rises 16 → 17.
- [`engine/tools/test_validate.py`](tools/test_validate.py) — 4 new tests for `health_check_overdue`: overdue past natural slot fires; silent at the natural-cadence slot; silent when the field is absent (legacy schema); silent when slots_since is below cadence.
- [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) — 4 new tests for the field bump: emit_report bumps `last_audit_session` and preserves other fields; emit_report adds the field when absent (legacy → new-schema transition); dry-run skips the bump; absent register_state.json yields a stderr warning without poisoning the audit. 188 tests total still pass; ruff + mypy --strict clean.
- [`engine/adr/0022-periodic-project-health-checks.md`](adr/0022-periodic-project-health-checks.md) — **Decision section + new Consequences amendment** recording the strict-modulo → overdue-catchup change at S-0041. Names the failure mode (silent slide of cadence-aligned slot consumption), the discovery surface (AI noticed only after user prompting), and the four-layer fix (register_state schema, hook, health_check.py, validate.py). Carriers updated list. Amendment-only per ADR 0036.
- [`engine/adr/0043-hook-architecture.md`](adr/0043-hook-architecture.md) — **Consequences amended** with the S-0041 logic change. The strict-modulo fix this ADR committed at S-0031 is acknowledged as having been the right correction at the time but introducing the silent-slide mode; the S-0041 amendment supersedes the strict-modulo logic without superseding the ADR's contract (the cadence-trigger surface and the two-layer recording mechanization).
- [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) — **cadence-trigger logic prose updated** with the overdue-catchup formula, the "due" / "overdue" surface split, and a new "History of the cadence-trigger logic" subsection summarizing the S-0001 → S-0030 / S-0031 → S-0041 / S-0041 onward evolution. The validator's `health_check_overdue` defense-in-depth role is named.
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — **Step 2 cadence-trigger prose rewritten** for overdue-catchup. The mirroring [`.claude/skills/session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md) updated identically.
- [`.claude/commands/start-engine.md`](../.claude/commands/start-engine.md) — **Step 2 prose updated** with the overdue-catchup formula and "due" / "overdue" surface text.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) — **new `health_check_overdue` soft-warn category entry** under "Soft-warns (signal, not blocker)." Names the defense-in-depth role, the SessionStart hook's overlap, the silent-skip behavior when the field is absent, and the recovery procedure (run the audit script — emit bumps the field — or document explicit deferral).
- [`engine/scheduled_audits.json`](scheduled_audits.json) — **S-0042 pushback/lesson tag adoption entry consumed.** The catch-up audit at S-0041 absorbed the check (Gaps section finding: zero adoption across S-0033 → S-0040). Entry moved from `audits` to a new `consumed_log` array preserving the audit trail. The file's `description` field updated to reflect the overdue-catchup logic per ADR 0022 amendment at S-0041.
- [`docs/health-checks/S-0041.md`](../docs/health-checks/S-0041.md) — **second project health check report.** 5 mechanical (post-rewrite) + 13 manual observations across the five categories. Headline finding: the strict-modulo cadence-trigger silent-slide bug. Meta-finding: the audit was itself the case study of its own concern — the AI authored the analysis at production quality but with too-narrow scope, then queued the recommended fixes for "future sessions" — exactly the silent-deferral pattern CLAUDE.md "Default to fix-in-context" targets. The user pushed back twice ("STOP PUSHING THINGS OFF"; "Why is audit dead weight not scanning every folder? Why are they opt in only scans?"); both pushbacks drove inline fixes to the audit's recommendations + the audit's own scope. Net: 0 follow-up items carried forward to STATE.md.

- [`engine/tools/sweep_worktrees.sh`](tools/sweep_worktrees.sh) — **counter-bug fix.** The pipe-to-while pattern `git worktree list ... | while read -r WT_PATH; do ... REMOVED=$((REMOVED + 1)); done` ran the loop body in a subshell, so per-iteration increments to `REMOVED` and `SKIPPED` were lost; the final `[sweep] removed N, skipped K` line silently reported "removed 0, skipped 0" despite the actual removals. Fixed by switching to process substitution `done < <(git worktree list ...)` so the loop runs in the parent shell. Discovered when the S-0041 sweep removed 37 stale worktrees but the script's tally line showed zeros.
- **stale worktree sweep applied: 37 removed.** `engine/tools/sweep_worktrees.sh --apply` removed every claude/* worktree whose branch was fully merged into main and whose working tree was clean. Two worktrees survived: `frosty-dijkstra-484bac` (this session's worktree) and `flamboyant-sanderson-a81ba1` (dirty working tree). Worktree count: ~39 → 2 active.
- [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) — **universal-scan rewrite of audit_dead_weight + audit_bloat + audit_gaps.** Per the second user pushback ("Why is audit dead weight not scanning every folder? Why are they opt in only scans?"), the three audit categories are rewritten from opt-in directory-specific scans to universal scans over all `.md` files under `REPO_ROOT` (filesystem walk, not `git ls-files`, so the synthetic-repo test fixtures still work). New constants: `DEAD_WEIGHT_SKIP_PATH_PREFIXES` (`.claude/`, `engine/tools/test_fixtures/`, `engine/session/archive/`, `docs/health-checks/`) and `DEAD_WEIGHT_SKIP_NAMES` (per-file skip-list with structural reasons). New helpers: `_list_scanned_md_files()`, `_last_touched_session(path)`, `_count_inbound_citations(path, all_md)`. **audit_dead_weight** scans every tracked .md for staleness (no S-NNNN commit reference newer than `PRODUCT_DOC_STALE_SESSIONS = 20` sessions ago) and inbound-citation count (count of other .md files mentioning the file's name); files that hit either signal land in the report. **audit_bloat** scans every tracked .md for line counts >`LARGE_DOC_LINES = 300`; renamed constant from `LARGE_OPS_DOC_LINES`. **audit_gaps** gains universal scans for TBD/TODO/FIXME markers in tracked .md files (with skip-list for files that *describe* the marker convention rather than *use* it as a live gap) and for `build_plan/*.md` chunks not yet referenced by any closed session's archive. Plus: `BUILD_PLAN_DIR` and `PRODUCT_DOCS_DIR` module-level constants added; the test fixture monkeypatches both so tests don't scan the real repo. The universal-scan rewrite caught the audit's own scope-too-narrow failure mode (the original opt-in scope let `prep-paideia-prompt-pack.md` go undetected for 24 sessions).
- [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) — **fixture monkeypatch added for `BUILD_PLAN_DIR` and `PRODUCT_DOCS_DIR`** (so universal scans don't hit the real repo from the synthetic-repo tests); **two test wording updates** (`no inbound citations` → `zero inbound citations` matching the rewritten message text). 188 tests pass; ruff + mypy --strict clean.

Subject: the AI-deferral lapse this audit surfaced and the user pushed back on; the failed approach + non-obvious reason + working fix become recoverable for future sessions per the convention's structural shape. `wing: paideia, room: lessons, drawer_id: drawer_paideia_lessons_1d6c3631798c29f60c7153fa`.

### Added (S-0039 — Structural-reference parser tool + ADR 0047)
- [`engine/adr/0047-structural-reference-parser-tool-and-adversarial-triage-workflow.md`](adr/0047-structural-reference-parser-tool-and-adversarial-triage-workflow.md) — **new engine ADR.** Settles four operational decisions for consuming the structural-reference class established by [ADR 0046](../product/adr/0046-structural-reference-posture-extends-to-philosophy-reference-works.md): (1) the parser is a standing engine tool decoupled from phases, runnable ad-hoc whenever a source is acquired; (2) it is document-agnostic with per-document-type heuristic configs (one parser, multiple input adapters sharing a structural-detector layer; configs name document type, not source); (3) output is signal-not-truth, ephemeral-not-persisted (recall-prioritized, LLM parametric knowledge as the credibility threshold, no `engine/parser_findings/` directory, no cross-source corroboration mechanism — reversibility named); (4) triage is adversarial, defaulting to rejection (three rejection filters: not in parametric knowledge, duplicates existing graph node, out-of-scope per [ADR 0001](../product/adr/0001-pedagogical-edges-not-historical.md)). Triage prompt template deferred to first-real-use. PDF input adapter deferred to first-PDF-source-acquisition. ADR 0046, ADR 0011, Generative Graph Independence all unchanged.
- `engine/tools/parse_structural_reference.py` — **new module.** Standing engine tool implementing ADR 0047. Module-top contract block enumerating responsibility families and non-responsibilities; pure-function structural detectors (`detect_entries`, `detect_cross_references`, `detect_section_path`, `detect_word_count`); `InputAdapter` interface with concrete `HTMLInputAdapter` for SEP-shaped HTML (entry boundary via `<title>` + first `<h1>`; cross-references via `<a>` matching `entries/[a-z-]+/?`; section path from TOC ancestry); `FocusingBriefEmitter` producing per-entry JSON with title, id, cross-references, section-path, word-count, page-or-url, extraction-confidence; per-document-type configs (`ENCYCLOPEDIA_CONFIG`); CLI dispatch via argparse (`--source`, `--document-type`, `--output`). Mirrors the architectural shape of [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py).
- `engine/tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py` — **new test suite.** One test class per detector (one test per logical branch), per adapter (happy-path + malformed-input), per emitter (schema correctness + confidence-score), plus integration tests against the SEP test fixtures and CLI tests via subprocess. Inherits the autouse `_scrub_git_env` fixture from [`engine/tools/conftest.py`](tools/conftest.py) per [ADR 0045](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md).
- `engine/tools/test_fixtures/sep/` — **new directory** holding 5–10 cached SEP entries' raw HTML acquired under SEP's explicit crawl-for-indexing permission per [`product/docs/content-strategy.md`](../product/docs/content-strategy.md) Tier 4. Topical diversity for cross-domain coverage testing. Parser-implementation-internal — never reach the production graph or any user-facing surface; ADR 0011 unchanged.
- `engine/tools/requirements.txt` — `beautifulsoup4>=4.12.0` added for the HTML input adapter. Future PDF adapter will add `pypdf` or `pdfplumber` at the session that lands it.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — **index entry added** for ADR 0047. Header count corrected from stale "11 ADRs total" (table already had 12) to "13 ADRs total — all Accepted." Full-collection count updated 44 → 47 (13 engine + 34 product).

- [`product/docs/content-strategy.md`](../product/docs/content-strategy.md) — **"Cross-Domain Reference Inventories — Survey" section populated** with per-candidate Tier 1, Tier 2, Tier 3, and Tier 4 assessments. Tier 1 evaluates the five known prerequisite-shaped candidates (Khan Academy knowledge map, ConceptNet `/r/HasPrerequisite`, university CS curriculum prerequisite graphs, Mathlib, Metamath set.mm) against the five usability axes with URL citations and adoption verdicts. New "Phase 5 consumer pointer" subsection cross-links to [ROADMAP §5.2](../ROADMAP.md). The "SEP as Structural Reference, Not Content Source" subsection extended in place with the class-extension cross-link to ADR 0046.
- [`product/adr/0046-structural-reference-posture-extends-to-philosophy-reference-works.md`](../product/adr/0046-structural-reference-posture-extends-to-philosophy-reference-works.md) — **new product ADR.** Settles that the structural-reference posture established for SEP extends to a class of curated philosophy reference works (IEP, Routledge Encyclopedia of Philosophy, Oxford Reference philosophy collection, Wikipedia). Distinguishes graph-shape value (cross-reference adjacency network and concept-inventory curation; load-bearing for Phase 5 seed authoring) from content/prose value (already parametrically accessible to Sonnet/Opus; addressed by [ADR 0011](../product/adr/0011-no-hosted-copyrighted-material.md) which remains unchanged). Notes EU sui generis database rights consideration for UK-published members (Routledge, Oxford). Reaffirms Generative Graph Independence: structural references are inputs to the generation pass, not the graph's substance. Source-acquisition decisions (paywalled members) remain per-session in the consuming Phase 5 sub-session.

### Added (S-0037 — Phase 4 graph validation per ADR 0016)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **`validate_graph()` flesh-out replacing the stub** per [ADR 0016](adr/0016-graph-construction-needs-live-validation.md) and the [Phase 4 build-readiness gate](build_readiness/phase_4_graph_validation.md). Connects to the live Supabase DB via `psycopg` (lazy import; service-role connection string consumed from `SUPABASE_DB_URL`). Three hard-fails: duplicate node IDs, dangling edge references (defense-in-depth — the schema FK at `0003_edges.sql:52-53` prevents inserts but the audit covers any post-restore window before constraints are validated), prerequisite cycles via Kosaraju SCC restricted to the `pedagogical_prerequisite` subgraph (other types may legitimately cycle). Seven soft-warn categories per gate T2-D — `undeclared_predicate`, `attribute_shape_inconsistency`, `missing_rigor_score`, `render_readiness_violation`, `synthetic_review_queue`, `orphan_leaf`, `suspicious_cross_domain_ratio` — registered in `checks_run` even when zero findings fire so cross-session telemetry distinguishes "category clean" from "category did not run." `--export-snapshot PATH` mode dumps full nodes-and-edges JSON for offline review (gate T2-F). Audit-skip path when `SUPABASE_DB_URL` unset records `graph_audit_skipped` and runs no DB query — non-seed-authoring sessions are not gated on connectivity. Default-mode validator check count rises 16 → 23 when env set (16 unchanged when unset). Module-level constants: `GRAPH_SOFT_WARN_CATEGORIES`, `SCAFFOLDING_TOKENS`, `CROSS_DOMAIN_RATIO_THRESHOLD = 0.40`, `ATTRIBUTE_SHAPE_MINORITY_THRESHOLD = 0.30`, `RIGOR_SCORE_DEFAULT = 0.5`, `PREREQUISITE_EDGE_TYPE = 'pedagogical_prerequisite'`, `PREDICATE_MANIFEST_PATH`, `SUPABASE_DB_URL_ENV`. Pure helper functions (testable without DB): `_read_predicate_manifest`, `_detect_duplicate_node_ids`, `_detect_dangling_edges`, `_detect_prerequisite_cycles`, `_detect_undeclared_predicates`, `_detect_attribute_shape_inconsistency`, `_detect_missing_rigor_score`, `_detect_render_readiness_violations`, `_detect_synthetic_review_queue`, `_detect_orphan_leaves`, `_detect_suspicious_cross_domain_ratio`, `_write_snapshot`. The DB-touching layer is a single function `_read_graph_from_db(connection_string)` that tests monkey-patch with fixture data.
- [`engine/tools/test_validate.py`](tools/test_validate.py) — **new test coverage for `validate_graph`** under `# validate_graph (Phase 4 implementation per ADR 0016 + gate ...)`. The `_node` and `_edge` factories build row dicts with the columns `validate_graph()` reads. **250 tests passing total** (was 202 before S-0037). ruff + mypy --strict clean.

### Added (S-0036 — Bash 3.2 fix + deferral-discipline guardrails)
- [`engine/tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py`](tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py) — **new audit script.** Diffs `HANDOFF.md` across this session's range (`<eager-claim-SHA>^..HEAD`) and finds every newly-added section header. Each must carry a `**Disposition:**` line in one of four forms: `fixed-in-session @ <SHA>`, `deferred-with-user-confirmation`, `out-of-scope`, `not-actionable`. Hard-fails at exit 2 if any new section is missing or has a malformed disposition. Wired into the pre-commit hook for `closing` mode so the close commit cannot land if any new HANDOFF section is undispositioned. Catches the deferral pattern named in CLAUDE.md "Default to fix-in-context."
- [`engine/tools/test_audit_handoff_dispositions.py`](tools/test_audit_handoff_dispositions.py) — **new test suite.** 29 tests covering `is_valid_disposition` (8 tests across all four valid forms + rejection cases including bare `fixed-in-session` without SHA and trailing prose after a known form), `_extract_disposition` (4 tests including first-match-wins and whitespace-stripping), `parse_added_sections` (7 tests covering empty diff, no-section diffs, single sections with/without disposition, multiple sections, edits to existing sections, and skipped diff metadata), `find_undispositioned_sections` (4 tests), plus 6 main()-integration tests via tmp_path git repos asserting exit codes 0/2 and stderr content for valid / missing-disposition / unrecognized-disposition / list-mode / existing-section-edit / no-eager-claim cases. ruff-format clean; mypy --strict clean.

### Changed (S-0036)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **persistent-warn aggregation refactored from associative arrays (bash 4+) to parallel indexed arrays (bash 3.2 portable).** The prior code used `declare -A CATEGORY_FIRINGS` and `${!CATEGORY_FIRINGS[@]}` for key iteration — both bash 4+ features. macOS ships `/bin/bash` 3.2; the shebang resolves to that, so the persistent-warn surface had been silently emitting "none above the 3-of-5 threshold" regardless of archive contents (today invisible because all recent archives carry zero soft-warns; would have suppressed real persistence detection). Replaced with parallel `CATEGORY_NAMES` + `CATEGORY_FIRINGS` indexed arrays plus a `_find_category_index` helper using a C-style for-loop. Verified on `bash 3.2.57` — hook runs clean, no `declare: -A: invalid option` error. The HANDOFF.md S-0035 entry queuing this fix is removed (resolved). Side discovery surfaced at S-0035 close; the original deferral was retroactively the wrong call per the new "Default to fix-in-context" posture rule.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **new "Default to fix-in-context" posture rule** under standing rules. Codifies that a bug found mid-session whose fix is in context defaults to inline fix; deferral requires user confirmation OR a named threshold (substantial scope / contract change / budget cap reached). Mechanically backstopped by the new disposition audit. No ADR per user direction at S-0036 — the contract layer stays light; CLAUDE.md is the load-bearing surface for session-internal posture rules.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) — **new closing-mode hard-fail block** invokes `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`. The close commit cannot land if any new HANDOFF.md section in the session lacks a valid disposition. Mirrors the gate-stack pattern (validate.py default + --code-gates + --sql-gates).
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **new step 6a "HANDOFF-disposition audit"** documents the audit, the four accepted disposition forms, and the resolution path (apply the fix in this session and use `fixed-in-session @ <SHA>`, OR get user confirmation and use `deferred-with-user-confirmation`). Notes that the audit also fires from pre-commit closing-mode so manual invocation is a way to catch issues before staging.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) — **mirror of step 6a** per ADR 0036/0044 doc → skill propagation discipline.
- [`HANDOFF.md`](../HANDOFF.md) — **bash 3.2 entry deleted** (resolved at S-0036 by the session-start.sh refactor).

### Added (S-0035 — Engine hardening for restart: subprocess env scrub + atomic mempalace + boot-time probes)
- [`engine/adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md`](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md) — **new ADR (engine).** Mechanizes four shared-state integrity rules in response to S-0033 (env-leak wrote `core.bare=true` to parent `.git/config`) and S-0034 (chromadb HNSW segment corruption crashed every subsequent session). Subprocess env scrubbing across all hooks + `validate.py`'s 4 code-gate subprocess calls; atomic `cp -a` snapshot + `probe_palace.py` verify + rollback wrapper around `mempalace hook run`; boot-time `validate.py --health-probe-only` invoked from `session-start.sh`; shutdown soft-warn aggregation changes from "final validator run only" to "max-count across all this-session `validate-history.jsonl` invocations" so boot-only probe firings reach the archive. Default-mode validator check count rises 14 → 16.
- [`engine/tools/scrub_env.py`](tools/scrub_env.py) — **new helper.** `scrubbed_env(base=None)` returns a copy of an env dict with every `GIT_*` key removed; `scrub_in_place(env)` mutates in place. Used by `validate.py` for subprocess `env=` parameter and by `probe_repo.py` for its own git subprocess calls.
- [`engine/tools/scrub_env.sh`](tools/scrub_env.sh) — **new bash helper.** Defines `scrub_git_env` function that unsets every `GIT_*` variable in the current shell. Sourced by all four hook scripts before they shell out. Portable across bash 3.2 and bash 4+.
- [`engine/tools/conftest.py`](tools/conftest.py) — **new pytest config.** Hoists the `_scrub_git_env` autouse fixture from `test_audit_side_discoveries.py` so the GIT_* env scrub applies to every test in the suite, not just the side-discovery tests. The original fixture remains in place — both running is idempotent.
- [`engine/tools/probe_palace.py`](tools/probe_palace.py) — **new probe script.** Opens chromadb `PersistentClient` at `~/.mempalace/palace`, lists collections, calls `get_collection() + count()` on each. Sub-second on a 130 MB palace. Exit codes: 0 healthy, 1 suspect, 2 hard-broken; SIGSEGV (139) is treated as hard-broken by callers — the S-0034 chromadb_rust_bindings signature. `MEMPALACE_PROBE_PALACE_PATH` env var override exists for testing.
- [`engine/tools/probe_repo.py`](tools/probe_repo.py) — **new probe script.** Checks worktree's effective `core.bare`, parent clone's standalone `.git/config` `core.bare` (catches the S-0033 worktree-override-masks-broken-parent case), HEAD resolution. Same exit-code convention as `probe_palace.py`.
- [`engine/tools/test_scrub_env.py`](tools/test_scrub_env.py) — **new test suite.** 11 tests covering both `scrubbed_env` and `scrub_in_place`: GIT_* removal, non-GIT preservation, source-dict immutability, explicit-base parameter, empty-dict handling, return-self-for-chaining.
- [`engine/tools/test_probe_palace.py`](tools/test_probe_palace.py) — **new test suite.** 4 tests: missing palace dir → suspect; empty palace dir → suspect or hard-broken; healthy palace via real chromadb → exit 0; findings emit on stderr.
- [`engine/tools/test_probe_repo.py`](tools/test_probe_repo.py) — **new test suite.** 5 tests: clean repo → exit 0; `core.bare=true` → exit 2 with hard-broken message; outside git repo → exit 2; findings emit on stderr; recovery message names correct path.

### Changed (S-0035)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **subprocess env scrubbing on all 4 code-gate calls** (ruff check, ruff format, mypy --strict, pytest at lines ~820, 830, 840, 873) — pass `env=scrubbed_env()`. **New `validate_shared_state_health()`** dispatches `probe_palace.py` and `probe_repo.py` as subprocesses, mapping exit codes 0/1/2/139 to `add_check` / `soft_warn` / `hard_fail`. Wired into the default check set so every pre-commit run includes shared-state checks. **New `--health-probe-only` flag** dispatches only the shared-state checks for the SessionStart hook's sub-second boot-time verification. **conftest.py exempted from test-presence rule** so it doesn't trigger a false-positive "no test file for conftest.py" hard-fail.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **shared-state health probe step added** between cadence trigger and persistent-warn surface. Runs `validate.py --health-probe-only`; surfaces healthy as one-liner, soft-warn as stderr block citing categories, hard-broken as a LOUD attention banner pointing at ADR 0045 for diagnostics. Hook still always exits 0 (a hard-broken state must remain diagnosable from within a session). **Sources `scrub_env.sh`** at the top so `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` runs against a clean env.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/post-state-edit.sh`](tools/hooks/post-state-edit.sh), [`engine/tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh`](tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh) — **source `scrub_env.sh` and call `scrub_git_env`** before their `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` calls (and `mempalace search` in the ADR-write hook). Defense-in-depth against future leaked `GIT_DIR` from any sub-agent or Skill context.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh`](tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh) — **atomic-write wrapper around `mempalace hook run`.** Pre-mine `cp -a` snapshot to `palace.pre-mine` plus parallel KG snapshot dir; invoke mempalace with scrubbed env; post-mine `probe_palace.py` verify; on healthy/suspect rotate snapshot to `palace.last-good` (one retained between hook fires); on hard-broken or SIGSEGV roll back palace + KG and force the hook's eventual EXIT_CODE non-zero so the next session's boot reading of `mempalace-hook.log` surfaces the rollback event. Snapshot semantics are byte-level (`cp -a`); minor inconsistency window from mid-WAL-write at snapshot time accepted because corruption recovery dwarfs that cost.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **step 8 amended** for the soft-warn aggregation change per ADR 0045 Decision 4: compute `outcome_summary_soft_warns` by max-count aggregation across every `validate.py` invocation in this session's `validate-history.jsonl` entries, not just the final pre-commit run. Schema example gains `chromadb_palace_health` and `repo_config_health` keys. Aggregation procedure spelled out (filter by session_id or timestamp window; per-category max).
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) — **mirror of the step 8 amendment** per ADR 0036/0044 doc → skill propagation discipline.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) — **two new soft-warn category entries** (`chromadb_palace_health`, `repo_config_health`) under "Soft-warns (signal, not blocker)" with recovery procedures. The hard-fail escalation (definite corruption blocks the commit) is documented inline so the suspicion / hard-broken split is clear.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **Posture vs machinery section narrows further** with three new mechanized rules (subprocess env scrubbing, mempalace atomic-write, boot-time shared-state probes) per ADR 0045.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — index entry added for ADR 0045.
- [`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md) — Current phase row appended with S-0035 close summary; Last build session row → S-0035 (engine hardening); Prior build session row → S-0034 (rolls in); Next session work item → S-0036 = Phase 4 graph validation (the work originally planned for S-0035, displaced by this hardening session). Build-readiness gate report at `engine/build_readiness/phase_4_graph_validation.md` is unchanged structurally — its slot reference now reads as S-0036.

### Added (S-0033 — Pre-commit STATUS-capture bug + side-discovery audit + scheduling-barrier fix)
- [`engine/tools/audit_side_discoveries.py`](tools/audit_side_discoveries.py) — **new tool** per [HANDOFF.md](../HANDOFF.md) Item 2. Session-shutdown audit gate that requires explicit disposition for follow-up markers in commit messages. Scans this session's commit-message text (range `<eager-claim-SHA>..HEAD`) for case-insensitive whole-word matches against `flagged`, `follow-up`, `follow up`, `TODO`, `FIXME`, `deferred`, `noted for`, `future session`, `next session`, `pending`, `out of scope`. Filters obvious negations preceded by `no` / `not` / `nothing` / `no longer` within ~12 chars. Matches each hit against the `side_discoveries` field in `engine/session/current.json`; exit 2 (hard-fail) on undispositioned markers, exit 0 if all matched or none found. CLI: `--range`, `--dispositions`, `--list` (dry-run). Layer 1 contract docstring per ADR 0038 + ADR 0039.
- [`engine/tools/test_audit_side_discoveries.py`](tools/test_audit_side_discoveries.py) — **new test suite** — 22 tests covering scan_markers (basic hit, case-insensitive, negation filter, distinct-phrases-in-one-commit, hyphenated vs spaced follow-up, context newline stripping), is_negated, match_dispositions (pairing by sha-prefix + marker, undispositioned-only, extra-dispositions ignored), load_dispositions (missing file, no field, marker normalization, non-list rejection), and main() integration via tmp_path git fixtures (no markers, undispositioned, all dispositioned, --list flag, --range override) plus find_eager_claim_sha and session_range. ruff-format clean; mypy --strict clean.

### Changed (S-0033)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) — **STATUS=$? capture bug fix** per HANDOFF.md Item 1. The three `if ! cmd; then STATUS=$?; ...` blocks (validate.py, --code-gates, --sql-gates) had been silently allowing hard-fails through because `$?` after a negated pipeline always evaluates to 0 (the negation's success). Replaced each block with the `STATUS=0; cmd || STATUS=$?` pattern, which preserves `set -e` semantics and captures cmd's actual exit code. Verified by smoke-test: a deliberate mypy --strict violation now blocks the commit (exit 1) where previously it was silently accepted. Also: **`engine/scheduled_audits.json` added to exploration-mode allowed-paths** per HANDOFF.md Item 3 — scheduling a near-term audit between sessions no longer requires opening a session. The hook docstring header is updated to list the new allowed path.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **new step 6 "Side-discovery audit"** inserted between ENGINE_LOG (step 5) and diary (renumbered to step 7) per HANDOFF.md Item 2. Hard-fail gate; the script does not introduce a new soft-warn category. Steps 7→8, 8→9, 9→10 renumbered; Recovery section step references updated; internal cross-references in steps 7/8 updated to point at the new step numbering.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) — **mirror of the new step 6** per ADR 0036/0044 doc → skill propagation discipline. Pre-existing Recovery-section step-number drift (steps 1–8 / step 7 / step 8 references that were already stale against the ops doc's 9-step numbering) corrected in passing.

### Added (S-0032 — MemPalace audit cleanup + improvements)
- [`engine/scheduled_audits.json`](scheduled_audits.json) — **new file** per the S-0032 MemPalace audit plan Improvement G near-term-audit mechanism. Each entry names a `trigger_session`, audit description, when added, and per what doc. Distinct from the cadence health check (ADR 0022; cadence 10 as of S-0033) — this surfaces one-time adoption checks tied to specific session-numbered triggers added by prior decisions. First entry: S-0042 audit of pushback/lesson tag adoption.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) — **"Project usage scope" section added** — names the surface this project uses from MemPalace's broad ~19-tool MCP surface (search, add_drawer, diary with `agent_name=claude`, read-only inspection) and what it explicitly does NOT use (KG, tunnels), with reasoning. Closes the "sessions making up usage on the fly" failure mode the S-0032 audit diagnosed. Also: "Known issues" section added documenting the `mempalace_graph_stats.total_rooms` undercount (cosmetic; trust taxonomy / CLI status for room counts). "Initialize against this repo" updated to no longer recommend `mempalace mine docs/` per Improvement E (the 88 existing operations-doc drawers can be cleaned up in a future session; the install procedure no longer recreates them).
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-tagging-conventions.md`](operations/mempalace-tagging-conventions.md) — **two new tag definitions** per Improvement G: `pushback` (verbatim moments where AI surfaced a real risk and user accepted the pushback, producing a course correction; partial mechanization of the trace-gap CLAUDE.md "Posture vs machinery" admits for the pushback rule) and `lesson` (procedural failures with non-obvious cause + working fix). Both manual via `mempalace_add_drawer`. Header bumped to "five tags." New "Room-targeting conventions" section codifies where each tag's drawers go: `decisions` for `decision`-tagged + `pushback`-that-crystallized; new `lessons` room for `lesson`-tagged; `s<NNNN>-<topic>` for session-meta; `general` for auto-captured `work`/`exploration` fallback; operations docs no longer mined as drawers.

### Changed (S-0032)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh`](tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh) — **PATH-fix for `mempalace` CLI resolution** — adds the same `~/Library/Python/3.9/bin/mempalace` fallback already present in `post-adr-write.sh` per ADR 0043. The wrapper invoked `mempalace hook run` directly without PATH resolution; Claude Code subshells inherit a narrowed PATH that does not include `~/Library/Python/3.9/bin/`, so the wrapper had been writing `FAIL exit=127` on every Stop and PreCompact event in worktree clones since S-0002 — silently, since the wrapper exits 0 to the harness regardless. The actual cause of the auto-capture breakage diagnosed at S-0032 (485 manual-MCP drawers exist; zero hook-driven captures despite Stop/PreCompact wiring). Verification at next Stop event: `.claude/logs/mempalace-hook.log` should show `OK exit=0` instead of `FAIL exit=127`.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh`](tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh) — **room-targeting check added** per Improvement B + Cleanup 3. The hook previously reported "drawer present" on any matching `decision`-tagged drawer regardless of room. Now distinguishes three cases: tag+id match AND result line names "paideia / decisions" → log OK silently; tag+id match AND only "paideia / general" lines present (legacy filing pattern) → emit migration reminder pointing at `mempalace_get_drawer` + `add_drawer` + remove/supersede; no tag+id match → emit existing two-layer recording reminder. Catches backslide at write time.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **scheduled-audit surface added** — new block reads `engine/scheduled_audits.json`, surfaces any entry whose `trigger_session` is at-or-before `next_id` (deferred audits keep firing until they land or the entry is removed). Default cadence in jq fallback updated 30 → 10 per the cadence-tightening below.
- [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) — **new audit category `audit_mempalace`** per Improvement D — fifth section in every audit report. Counts decisions-room drawers vs ADRs (two-layer recording compliance), `pushback`/`lesson` tag adoption (with Tags-line filtering to avoid false positives from operations docs that *describe* the tags), diary discipline via `diary_skipped` soft-warn aggregation across last 10 archives. Resolves CLI binary via the same fallback pattern used by hooks per ADR 0043. Graceful degradation when binary absent or daemon unreachable. Also: `cadence` field default 30 → 10; `detect_cadence` default 30 → 10; module docstring updated to name five categories. 16 new tests added; pytest 62/62 passing; ruff + mypy --strict clean.
- [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) — **new test coverage** for `audit_mempalace`, `_resolve_mempalace_binary`, `_run_mempalace`, `_count_adrs`, plus updated `test_detect_cadence_default` to expect 10. Tests use canonical module imports (shutil, subprocess, Path) for monkeypatching to satisfy mypy --strict.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **new step 6 "Write session diary entry"** inserted between ENGINE_LOG (step 5) and outcome_summary (renumbered to step 7) per Improvement F. Build sessions only; default-mode skip. agent_name=claude; 150-400 words first-person reflection. Skipped writes record `diary_skipped: 1` in outcome_summary_soft_warns; ADR 0042's 3-of-5 threshold catches drift automatically. - **MemPalace state changes (not git-tracked):** 10 ADR-companion drawers migrated from `general` room to `decisions` room via `mempalace_update_drawer` MCP calls. IDs: drawer_paideia_general_{728f310448ac608078a89932 (ADR 0037), 89eaa4e70c1b0581422a8381 (ADR 0036), 680ccb1932c659fc86c72938 (ADR 0035), b0bf9b7cc2e14fe97e6fd515 (ADR 0034), 43b28d4bbab2382f44196600 (ADR 0033), 1702dff6411b62f3b82d7be6 (ADR 0032), b729dee479daa86df6cb05ac (S-0007 ADR), 60eb2be239b7a77e36b43a47 (S-0021 ADR), c60ea1d65441eb20cf7420fa (ADR 0031), 00f446ee5114fff04974cd35 (S-0024 decision)}. Decisions room: 45 → 55 drawers. General room: 340 → 330 drawers. Drawer IDs retain `_general_` prefix because `update_drawer` doesn't regenerate IDs; the room field is what the post-adr-write hook now checks.

### Added (S-0031 — Session β: harness mechanization)
- [`engine/adr/0043-hook-architecture.md`](adr/0043-hook-architecture.md) — **new ADR (engine).** Commits to three new non-blocking Claude Code hooks under `engine/tools/hooks/`: `post-adr-write.sh` (PostToolUse on ADR writes; queries MemPalace for a `decision`-tagged drawer matching the ADR id; emits stderr reminder when none found — soft enforcement of the two-layer decision recording rule), `session-start.sh` (SessionStart event; computes the cadence-trigger modulus using the corrected `next_id mod cadence == 0` logic; reads last 5 archives for the persistent-warn surface per ADR 0042's 3-of-5 threshold; calibration window in effect until 5 structured archives accumulate), `post-state-edit.sh` (PostToolUse on STATE.md edits; verifies "Last build session" row populated and "Next session work item" block non-empty; surfaces reminders for placeholder tokens). All three exit 0 unconditionally — non-blocking by design — and log per-clone failures to `.claude/logs/<hook-name>.log`. Paired with the cadence-trigger off-by-one fix surfaced by the S-0030 audit. CLAUDE.md "Posture vs machinery" section narrows: two-layer decision recording, STATE.md required-fields verification, and the cadence trigger move from posture to soft-enforced machinery; pushback rule, startup-ceremony order, and Skill invocation remain posture.
- [`engine/adr/0044-skill-conversion-recipe-vs-reference.md`](adr/0044-skill-conversion-recipe-vs-reference.md) — **new ADR (engine).** Commits to converting recipe-shaped operations docs (`session-build-lifecycle.md`, `session-shutdown-sequence.md`, `build-readiness-gate.md`) to user-defined Skills under `.claude/skills/` with `disable-model-invocation: true`. Reference-shaped ops docs (escalation-criteria, code-discipline, migration-discipline, expression-contract-instantiation, tools-validate-interpretation, mempalace-*, adr-authoring, document-voice, health-check, cascade-discipline, soft-warn-lifecycle, cross-references) explicitly NOT converted — consulted repeatedly during work, not invoked as a unit. Partition criterion: a doc converts to a Skill iff the AI consumes it as a top-to-bottom procedure at a discrete moment (read-once, follow-in-order, exit when done); a doc stays a doc iff the AI consumes it at multiple junctures and extracts case-relevant rules. The ops doc remains the Layer 1 source-of-truth under [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md); the skill body adapts the same procedure into skill voice. Updates flow doc → skill, never the reverse.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh`](tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh) — **new hook script** per ADR 0043. Matches Edit/Write tool calls touching `(engine|product)/adr/NNNN-kebab-title.md`; queries `mempalace search` (resolves the user-scope binary at `~/Library/Python/3.9/bin/mempalace` if not on PATH); checks for a result whose body carries both a `**Tags:** ... decision` line and a mention of the ADR id; emits stderr reminder when no match. Non-blocking; logs to `.claude/logs/post-adr-write.log`.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **new hook script** per ADR 0043. Parses `next_id` from `register_state.json`, computes `next_id mod cadence == 0` (corrected from the original `last_claimed mod` off-by-one), emits cadence-trigger surface when modulus zero. Reads last 5 `engine/session/archive/S-NNNN.json` files; aggregates per-category soft-warn firings; surfaces categories firing in 3-of-5. Defers the surface during the calibration window (<5 structured archives). Non-blocking; logs to `.claude/logs/session-start.log`.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/post-state-edit.sh`](tools/hooks/post-state-edit.sh) — **new hook script** per ADR 0043. Matches Edit/Write tool calls touching `engine/STATE.md`; verifies the "Last build session" row in the `## Current` table is populated and the `## Next session work item` block has substantive content (>= 50 non-whitespace chars, no `<TBD>` / `<placeholder>` / `<fill ...>` tokens). Surfaces stderr reminders for any violation. Non-blocking; logs to `.claude/logs/post-state-edit.log`.
- [`.claude/skills/session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md) — **new user-defined Skill** per ADR 0044. Frontmatter: `name`, `description` (action-focused), `disable-model-invocation: true`. Body: boot procedure (read STATE.md, cadence trigger, persistent-warn surface, MemPalace query, build-readiness report check, eager-claim ritual, in-session cadence and push policy, recovery paths) adapted from the Layer 1 ops doc into skill voice.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) — **new user-defined Skill** per ADR 0044. Body: close procedure (audit, spot-check, cold-context review for Python and SQL, STATE.md + ENGINE_LOG updates, outcome_summary + structured outcome_summary_soft_warns, archive, final commit + FF + push, partial closure handling, interrupted-shutdown recovery).
- [`.claude/skills/build-readiness-gate/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/build-readiness-gate/SKILL.md) — **new user-defined Skill** per ADR 0044. Body: gate procedure (read chunk + ADRs, three Explore agents in parallel, Tier 1/2/3 triage, Tier 1 user resolution, source-document citation pass, cold-review pass against citations, build-readiness report write).

### Added (S-0029 — Infrastructure-misfire sweep, foundations)
- [`engine/adr/0041-cascade-analysis-discipline.md`](adr/0041-cascade-analysis-discipline.md) — **new ADR (engine).** Commits to a cascade-analysis discipline composed of three soft-warn validator checks (superseded-ADR-citation currency, ADR back-reference orphan, ADR Consequences-deliverable audit) plus manual procedures for the slice the validator cannot mechanize (file rename, ADR supersession, ops-doc restructure, deliverable handshake). Annotation mechanism `Orphan-OK` suppresses the orphan check on intentional load-bearing-future-work ADRs.
- [`engine/adr/0042-soft-warn-lifecycle-archive-canon.md`](adr/0042-soft-warn-lifecycle-archive-canon.md) — **new ADR (engine).** Moves trend canon from gitignored per-clone `engine/tools/validate-history.jsonl` to committed `engine/session/archive/S-NNNN.json` field `outcome_summary_soft_warns`. Boot-time persistent-warn surface (3-of-5 archives) at `/start-engine`. Escalation criterion at 10 consecutive archives (promote-to-hard-fail / accept-and-annotate / address-inline).
- [`engine/operations/cascade-discipline.md`](operations/cascade-discipline.md) — **new Layer 1 source-of-truth** for [ADR 0041](adr/0041-cascade-analysis-discipline.md). Mechanical checks summary, manual cascade procedures, lifecycle integration into shutdown spot-check + build-readiness-gate triage, Orphan-OK annotation mechanism.
- [`engine/operations/soft-warn-lifecycle.md`](operations/soft-warn-lifecycle.md) — **new Layer 1 source-of-truth** for [ADR 0042](adr/0042-soft-warn-lifecycle-archive-canon.md). Source-of-truth migration (jsonl → archive structured field), boot-time surface algorithm, closing-discipline integration, escalation-criterion details, migration-window acknowledgment for pre-ADR archives.
- [`engine/operations/cross-references.md`](operations/cross-references.md) — **new engine-side dependency map.** Companion to `product/docs/CROSS_REFERENCES.md`. Maps engine ADRs (0016, 0022, 0036, 0037, 0038, 0039, 0040, 0041, 0042) to consumers; operations docs to consumers; tools to consumers; harness to consumers.
- [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) — **new producer script** per [ADR 0022](adr/0022-periodic-project-health-checks.md), authored under [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md) three-layer code-discipline contract. Aggregates audit data per the four health-check.md categories (Fit, Gaps, Dead weight, Bloat) and emits a populated report at `docs/health-checks/S-NNNN.md`. CLI: `--session S-NNNN [--dry-run]`. Reads committed sources only (does NOT query MemPalace per documented non-responsibility). 45 pytest tests passing; ruff + ruff-format + mypy --strict clean. Closes the deliverable promised in ADR 0022 Consequences (originally anticipated "around S-0025").
- [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) — **new test suite** for health_check.py. 45 tests covering `CategoryFindings` accumulator, archive helpers (list_archives, read_archive, soft_warns_from_archive), four audit functions across clean/dirty/empty input paths, report rendering, cadence detection, and CLI exit-code paths.
- [`docs/health-checks/`](../docs/health-checks/) — **new directory at repo root.** Straddles the engine/product wall (per [ADR 0037](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md) edge case, same as CLAUDE.md and HANDOFF.md). [`docs/health-checks/README.md`](../docs/health-checks/README.md) explains the directory + workflow. [`docs/health-checks/TEMPLATE.md`](../docs/health-checks/TEMPLATE.md) carries the report shape for contributors to copy-and-fill (mirrors `engine/operations/health-check.md` template with the new ADR 0041/0042 categories).
- **Three new soft-warn validator checks** in [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) per [ADR 0041](adr/0041-cascade-analysis-discipline.md): `validate_superseded_adr_currency` (greps tracked .md files outside */adr/* and ENGINE_LOG.md/CHANGELOG.md for citations of Superseded ADRs without historical marker), `validate_adr_back_reference_orphan` (Accepted ADRs with zero non-ADR citations, Orphan-OK suppression), `validate_adr_consequences_deliverable_audit` (heuristic regex against ADR Consequences sections for closed-session-promised paths absent on disk; resolves both repo-root-relative and ADR-directory-relative). Helper `_tracked_md_files` walks rglob with .git/.claude/worktrees skip. 14 new pytest tests covering clean/dirty/suppression/exclusion paths. Total pytest 115 passing.
